Regulations for Primary and Secondary Schools and Normal Schools (7)

Article 108: The principal of a senior middle school must be of sound character and outstanding talent. In addition to possessing the qualifications stipulated in the preceding article, they must also meet one of the following qualifications:

(1) Having served as a professor or full-time lecturer in a liberal arts, science, or education college or department of a national university for more than one year;

(2) Having held a senior position in a provincial or directly-administered municipal education administrative agency for more than two years with outstanding achievements;

(3) Having served as the principal of a junior middle school for more than three years with outstanding achievements;

Article 109: A person with one of the following circumstances shall not be employed as a middle school principal: (1) Convicted of a criminal offense with conclusive evidence; (2) Having failed to complete handover procedures as a public official; (3) Having mediocre performance as a principal or educational administrator; (4) Suffering from mental illness or a chronic illness that prevents them from performing their duties; (5) Engaging in improper behavior or having bad habits;

Article 110: Senior middle school teachers must be of sound character, and the subject they teach must be the subject they specialize in. They must also meet one of the following qualifications:

(1) Having passed the senior middle school teacher examination or assessment;

(2) Graduating from a domestic or foreign normal university;

(3) Having at least one year of teaching experience after graduating from a domestic or foreign university undergraduate program, higher normal undergraduate program, or specialized course;

(4) Having at least two years of teaching experience after graduating from a domestic or foreign junior college or specialized school undergraduate program;

(5) Having published valuable specialized writings;

Article 111: Junior middle school teachers must be of sound character, and the subject they teach must be the subject they specialize in. They must also meet one of the following qualifications:

(1) Having passed the junior middle school teacher examination or assessment; (2) Possessing one of the qualifications stipulated for senior middle school teachers; (3) Graduating from a domestic or foreign university undergraduate program, higher normal undergraduate program, or specialized course; (4) Having at least one year of teaching experience after graduating from a domestic or foreign junior college or specialized school undergraduate program; (5) Having at least three years of teaching experience after graduating from a school equivalent to a senior middle school level and having definite research achievements in the subject they teach; (6) Possessing refined skills (specifically applicable to industrial arts teachers);

Article 112: A person with one of the following circumstances shall not be employed as a middle school teacher: (1) Convicted of a criminal offense with conclusive evidence; (2) Having poor performance; (3) Neglecting duties; (4) Being negligent in education and school affairs; (5) Suffering from mental illness or a chronic illness that prevents them from performing their duties; (6) Engaging in improper behavior or having bad habits;

Article 113: Middle school teachers who have continuously served in one school for nine years may take a one-year sabbatical to engage in research and investigation and must submit their results to the school for direct submission to the provincial or municipal education administrative agency or submit them through the county or municipal education administrative agency to the provincial education department for review. Teachers on sabbatical as mentioned in the preceding paragraph shall continue to receive their original salary, but only if they do not hold any other paid positions;

Article 114: The education administrative agencies of each province and city shall strive to facilitate the further education of middle school teachers and formulate measures to be submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval and implementation;

Article 115: The assessment, employment, and protection of middle school teachers shall be determined by separate regulations;

Article 116: The salary grade table and annual merit pay measures for teachers of provincial, municipal, and county middle schools shall be stipulated by the competent education administrative agency and submitted directly or transferred to the Ministry of Education for approval and implementation. Private middle schools shall refer to the conditions of public middle schools in each province and city and stipulate them in their school regulations. The lowest grade of the salary grade table for the preceding paragraph of teachers should refer to the local economic conditions and use the standard that can definitely maintain a suitable life;

Article 117: Middle school principals shall receive a salary three to five grades higher than full-time teachers, as determined by the competent education administrative agency or school board;

Article 118: The pension and death benefit measures for middle school teachers and staff shall be handled in accordance with the School Teachers and Staff Pension and Death Benefit Regulations promulgated by the National Government;

Chapter 13 Supplementary Provisions

Article 119: These Regulations may be amended by the Ministry of Education when necessary;

Article 120: These Regulations shall come into effect on August 1, 1933 (End of Middle School Regulations);

Regulations for Normal Schools

Chapter 1 General Provisions

Article 1: These Regulations are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 16 of the Normal School Law;

Article 2: A normal school is a place for rigorously training the minds and bodies of young people and cultivating sound elementary school teachers. In accordance with the provisions of Article 1 of the Normal School Law, the following trainings shall be implemented: (1) Strengthening physical fitness; (2) Cultivating moral character; (3) Fostering national culture; (4) Enriching scientific knowledge; (5) Cultivating diligent habits; (6) Inspiring interest in research on children's education; (7) Cultivating the spirit of lifelong service to education;

Article 3: A normal school may be affiliated with a special normal course and a kindergarten normal course. A public middle school and a senior middle school may also be affiliated with a special normal course;

Article 4: A normal school that exclusively enrolls female students is called a women's normal school. A normal school that focuses on cultivating teachers for rural elementary schools may be called a rural normal school;

Article 5: The length of study in a normal school is three years. The length of study in a kindergarten normal course is three or two years. The length of study in a special normal course is one year;

Article 6: In order to urgently cultivate teachers for compulsory education, various localities may establish simple normal schools or attach simple normal courses to normal schools and public junior middle schools. The measures shall be stipulated in separate chapters;

Article 7: The age of admission to a normal school is from 15 to 22 years old;

Chapter Two: Establishment and Management

Article 8: The establishment, relocation, and closure of Normal Schools established by provinces and municipalities (referring to municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan) should first be proposed by the provincial and municipal education administrative organs, with plans or reasons presented, and implemented after being reported to and approved by the Ministry of Education. The establishment, alteration, and closure of Normal Schools established by counties or jointly by counties should first be proposed by the competent education administrative organs, with plans or reasons presented, and implemented after being reported to and approved by the provincial education department, and the department should report to the Ministry for record. If Normal Schools fail to follow the procedures stipulated in the preceding paragraph, the higher-level education administrative organ may revoke them.

Article 9: Normal Schools should be established in cities or rural areas according to local conditions, and should be established in rural areas as much as possible within the feasible range.

Article 10: Each provincial education department may, according to the conditions of its province, divide the entire province into several normal school districts. Each normal school district may establish one Normal School and one Women's Normal School. The Normal Schools mentioned in the preceding paragraph should first recruit students from the counties within the district.

Article 11: Provincial Normal Schools shall be named after the location where they are situated. County Normal Schools shall be directly referred to as the County Normal School of a certain county. If there are two or more Normal Schools of the same type in one location, they may be distinguished by numerical order or by the name of a smaller area. Jointly established Normal Schools shall be called the Joint Normal School of several counties.

Article 12: Normal Schools shall, within one month after the beginning of the first academic semester each year, submit the following items to the competent education administrative organ for forwarding to the Ministry of Education for record: (1) List of new students, transfer students at all levels, returning students, suspended students, dropouts, and students at all levels for the current academic year; (2) Academic qualifications, positions, salaries, full-time or part-time status of the principal and faculty members for the current academic year; (3) Budget for the current fiscal year; (4) Changes in school regulations, school buildings, and equipment for the current academic year; (5) Academic performance reports of students at all levels for the previous academic year; (6) Final accounts or income and expenditure items for the previous fiscal year; (7) Service status and school guidance status of graduates from previous years.

Article 13: Normal Schools shall, within one month after the beginning of the second academic semester, submit the following items to the competent education administrative organ for forwarding to the Ministry of Education for record: (1) List of new students, transfer students at all levels, returning students, suspended students, and dropouts for the current semester; (2) Academic qualifications, experience, positions, salaries, full-time or part-time status of newly appointed faculty members for the current semester, names of faculty members who have left office and the reasons for leaving; (3) Academic performance reports of students at all levels for the previous semester.

Article 14: Two months before each graduation, Normal Schools shall prepare a list of the resumes and academic records of graduating students and submit it directly or through the provincial and municipal education administrative organs for approval before holding the graduation examination.

Article 15: Within one month after each graduation, Normal Schools shall prepare a graduation transcript of graduates and measures for service assignment and submit it directly or through the provincial and municipal education administrative organs for forwarding to the Ministry of Education for record.

Article 16: Each semester, the provincial and municipal education administrative organs shall dispatch supervisors to Normal Schools for inspection and guidance at least once, and the inspection and suggestions shall be reported to the Ministry of Education for review within one month after the completion of the inspection.

Chapter Three: Funding

Article 17: The start-up, regular, and temporary expenses of provincial and municipal Normal Schools shall be provided by provincial and municipal funds. The expenses of county or jointly established Normal Schools shall be provided by county funds or the funds of the counties jointly establishing the schools.

Article 18: County Normal Schools may receive provincial subsidies if they are indeed located in impoverished areas and have excellent performance.

Article 19: The standards for provincial subsidies to county Normal Schools shall be stipulated by the provincial education department and reported to the Ministry of Education for record.

Field Service Training Outline, as Supplementary Curriculum, and Stipulating Training Period for Compliance, 5. University Students in This City

Actively Organize Student Associations

丨A Conversation Meeting of University Representatives Was Held Yesterday丨

丨It is Set to Hold a Promoters' Meeting on the 30th of This Month丨

The University Student Association of this city, since the January 28th Shanghai War, has seen its organization fall into stagnation due to the scattering of students from various schools. Now, students from various schools, recognizing the growing national crisis and deepening anxieties, feel that the association has a real need to reorganize in a sound manner, in order to take unified steps to enrich the power of resistance. Therefore, at 2 PM yesterday afternoon, at the Shanghai Municipal Education Association hall on Avenue Foch, a conversation meeting of student representatives from various universities was convened.

Representatives Present: Daxia: Liu Xuru, Zhou Gongnan, Zhang Ruli; Soochow Law School: Xue Guangqian, Wang Qipei, Ren Xianqun; Fudan: Mo Xuanyuan, Chen Ruiheng; Jiaotong: Yuan Bingnan, Zhang Lie; Guanghua: Zhang Zixiu, Tao Yingjie; Chih Chih: Gu Jiwu, Shen Xinzhen, Zhang Guoliang, Wu Xi; Business School: He Xueni; Datong: Fang Jinan; Jiangnan: Guo Zengcheng, Hong Yousheng; Xinhua Art School: Pan Xingzhong; Culture: Sun Pian, Qian Kezhen, Hou Ji; Sino-French Institute of Technology: Liang Meichu; and more than 20 representatives from more than ten schools.

Steps Taken: The meeting began at 2 PM, with Xue Guangqian of Soochow elected as chairman and Mo Xuanyuan of Fudan as recorder. First, the chairman reported on the reasons for initiating the university association, the process of convening the conversation meeting, and the organizational situation of student associations in various schools. Then, representatives exchanged opinions and decided on the following steps: (1) The representatives attending the conversation meeting will jointly initiate and convene a meeting of promoters of the university association to produce a preparatory committee and formally establish the university association; (2) The promoters' meeting is scheduled for 2 PM on the 30th of this month at the Tianhou Palace; (3) The required expenses will be jointly borne by the attending schools; (4) Fudan, Jiaotong, and Daxia were nominated to be responsible for handling all matters related to convening the promoters' meeting.

New Initiatives at Chih Chih College

Since its establishment, Chih Chih College on the Shuishui Electric Road in Zhabei has been through nine years. Regarding academic matters: (1) After the thesis grades of graduates are evaluated by the director professor, the academic affairs meeting will select the top three, with the first place receiving a prize of 60 yuan, the second place 40 yuan, and the third place 20 yuan; (2) Any student with the best academic performance and pure conduct may, after being approved by the academic affairs meeting, be admitted to the next semester completely free of charge, and the next best may be exempted from tuition; (3) Any student who has never been absent from class during a semester will have three points added to their overall average grade, and those with less than ten hours of absence will have one point added. Regarding student extracurricular activities, the four professors Shen Yizhen, Ding Wenbiao, Zhang Zhongying, and Wu Hanfang were specially recommended to guide everything. Education Bureau Submits to Municipal Government for Approval

Cheng Yize's Letter States

Liu Changchun Can Come to Shanghai

Intends to Obtain a Position in Shanghai

Hoping for Assistance from All Sectors

Mr. Liu Changchun, the only athlete representing the country at the World Games, currently resides in Beiping. He feels that the local environment is not good and fears that his original talent may be worn away and submerged due to a lack of practice. He intends to find a place to stay in Shanghai, so that he can learn from and improve with famous athletes in East China. He has sent letters to various friends in Shanghai, asking for introductions. Mr. Cheng Yize, a famous and enthusiastic sportsman in this city, is also one of those entrusted. Mr. Cheng called this museum yesterday, stating the reason for Mr. Liu's coming to Shanghai, and hoping that all sectors will lend a helping hand, so that Mr. Liu will not be disappointed. The original letter is as follows: Sirs, recently I received a letter from Mr. Liu Changchun, the only athlete representing our country at the World Games, from Beiping. He deeply feels the bleakness of the sports circles there and the lack of opportunities and interest in practice, and fears that his personal useful talent will be worn away and submerged in the long run, which is a misfortune for the sports circles of our China. Therefore, he is eager to pack his bags and come here to learn from and improve with famous athletes in East China, hoping to receive the effect of other mountains. His ambition is far-reaching, his heart is long, and he is humble. His words do not abandon my own mediocrity, and he wants me to find him a place to stay to maintain his livelihood. In our country's sports circles, which are still in their infancy, at this time of global life panic, every talent often leaves school due to food and clothing, and then gradually degenerates, which is very regrettable. Now, even an athlete as agile as Mr. Liu cannot escape this example. I thought again and again, and I was eager to place Mr. Liu in an appropriate position, so that his skills can soar, and he can fulfill his strengths. But my current situation is different from the past, and there is no suitable position to accommodate Mr. Liu for a while, and I can't bear to leave it alone. My heart is uneasy and I can't control myself, so I specifically ask you to publish my letter, so that comrades in this city may be able to lend a helping hand, so that Mr. Liu can have no worries about living and can gain the benefits of learning in practice. In the future, those who gallop in the battlefield and vent their anger for my Chinese athletes are not only what I, one person, look forward to. If any of you readers have any advice, please send a letter or visit my residence on Matthew Hedgestone Road for a chat. Thank you very much.

Western Union Football

Western Police Win Over Youyou

Result Eight to Three

Today Youyou Battles Jinan

丨3 PM at Yiyuan丨

The Youyou football team fought the Western Police at the Yiyuan Stadium yesterday. Two or three thousand people watched. Youyou goalkeeper Liang Guanlian has not recovered since his wrist was fractured in the battle with Lax at Hongkou Park a few days ago. Yesterday, Wang Caigao played in his place. Veteran forwards Ye Jinjin and Shi Jinsheng were also unable to play due to injuries. Yesterday, Lu Shifang and Mao Honggui were substituted. As a result, the forward strength was reduced, and Huang Ruihua also did not perform well, so the forwards could not respond, and the rear could not defend. Then, the Western Police won with a score of eight to three. The battle record yesterday is as follows.

Youyou Misses an Opportunity Once The Western Police kicked off and attacked first, approaching step by step. Jack tried a shot, and Wang Caigao saved it. Xi Qiaosheng sent the ball to the right. Chen Guangyi invaded along the side, rushed to the side of the goal, and shot hard at the goal. Western Police goalkeeper Bradly fell to the ground and pounced out, Chen added another kick, the ball brushed the door and crossed to the left, Sun Jinshun, fired again, into a corner kick, Chen Guangyao sent it out, and failed again.

Western Police Scores Two Goals in a Row After escaping danger, the Western Police led their troops to counterattack. Pete's pass was excellent, and De Fei greeted it with his head, hitting the corner of the goal squarely, which was very clear. Only ten minutes had passed since the start of the game. In the center kick-off, the Western Police went deep again, and the Youyou rear was in a rather scattered state. Turner passed the ball in front of the goal, and Pete shot it into the net. The two goals were less than two minutes apart.

Youyou Returns Two Goals After losing two goals, Youyou's morale was greatly boosted and their spirits were uplifted. Sun Jinshun's two shots were both saved. Li Shiyou dribbled the ball and advanced again, but was blocked by the enemy. However, the two defenders of the Western Police let each other save the ball, and Xi Qiaosheng reaped the benefits, stepping forward and shooting, succeeding in one fell swoop. Therefore, Youyou's momentum was strong, and the Western Police's goal was in constant danger. Sun Jinshun forced a corner kick, Li Shiyou's kick was good, but it did not yield any benefits. Then, Huang Ruihua passed the ball to the left, and Li Shiyou returned it to the front of the goal, Hu Youcheng kicked it successfully, shooting into the corner of the goal, making the score two to two.

Unexpectedly, Three More Cities Were Lost After tying the score at two to two, it was generally believed that Youyou could win. Unexpectedly, the Western Police refused to show weakness and were aggressive, and their arrogance was very high. Within a quarter of an hour, Youyou lost three more cities in a row. The Western Police took the lead with five to two, ending the first half. The shooters of the Western Police were (1) De Fei, (3) Pete, (3) Parker. As for the reason why Youyou lost, it was due to the fact that the rear could not connect and the formation was scattered.

Western Police Scores Two More Goals At the beginning of the second half, the Youyou front showed even more signs of depression. Chen Guangyao was ambushed on the border and was frustrated. Xi Qiaosheng and Hu Youcheng were quite negligent, Li Shiyou was trapped by the enemy, and Sun Jinshun was unable to do anything alone. Therefore, the Youyou rear was extremely tight, and the enemy's traces were densely distributed in front of the goal. After ten minutes of stalemate, Pete shot a side ball, De Fei rushed in, and the Western Police added another goal. After Parker missed two shots, Jack also rushed in a goal, making the score seven to two.

Iron Foot Shoots Through the Willow Under the threat of violence, Youyou had few opportunities to move. Only Chen Guangyao once had the opportunity to attack the goal, but because he was too hasty and his steps were not accurate, he shot wildly. Sun Tiezu felt hurt by the scene and struggled single-handedly, ignoring everything, charging left and right, and got the ball to shoot 25 yards away from the goal. It was almost a last resort to make a desperate gamble. Unexpectedly, the ball's path was excellent, hitting the corner of the goal squarely, and he was overjoyed. But before long, Western Police's Parker scored another goal, ending the game with a score of eight to three. The lineup is as follows.

Western Police

Bradly, Gregson, Shaw, France, Gash, Stogges, Turner, De Fei, Parker, Jack, Pete

Youyou

Spring and Autumn

Suicide and Dreams

— Si Su

The world of the twentieth century is, after all, not the ancient times. In ancient times, people did not know each other, and there was no "each other." Asia did not know there was Europe, and Europe did not know there was America. Even within the same Asia, most Chinese people could not clearly know there was India, but vaguely thought there was a Western Paradise. It was not easy for people like Bodhidharma from India to come to China, and it also became a historical adventure for people like Faxian and Xuanzang to go to India. Therefore, even neighboring countries like Japan were vaguely regarded as a paradise; it was not until the Six Dynasties that it became clear that it was also a country inhabited by humans. However, the relationship between the two sides was still subtle, only that Emperor Gao of Qi granted King Wu of Wa the title of General Who Pacifies the East. What era is it now! Even if Japan relies on its strength and believes that no one can harm it, and intends to turn the clock back to the ancient times and swallow China alone, just like the Yuan and Qing dynasties entering the Central Plains, no other continents or countries have ever interfered. However, the wheel of time only moves forward and does not retreat. Japan should regret that it became strong too late and did not catch up with the Yuan and Qing dynasties, or even earlier, before the Liao and Jin dynasties. Today, to try to turn the wheel of time backward is, in fact, impossible. Although it is strong, it is still only "relying on itself." Although it is implementing a reversal, it is still only "intending." When a financial crisis occurs in the United States, it is entirely the United States' own business, but the impact has reached far and wide, and no major city has not been affected. Today's world is largely one where a single hair can move the whole body. Even a small matter, as long as it is international in nature, can absolutely not be shut out. How much more so is the major event of swallowing China alone? Moreover, the complexity of the international situation within China is more dramatic than anywhere else in the world. Japan, relying solely on "self-reliance" and "intending" to follow in the footsteps of the Yuan and Qing dynasties, swallowing China alone and not allowing third-party interference; isn't this "self-reliance" and "intending" equal to "suicide" and "dreams"!

書聲

— 啟楣

Every time I walk past the gate of a private school, there's always a chorus of voices reciting from books, so noisy that it's impossible to make out a single word.

I remember when I was a child in a private school. This noisy recitation had one unique use. The tutor was an old man, frail and stooped. All day long, apart from the unavoidable lecturing and circling of characters, most of his time was spent on the bed. But he wasn't fast asleep; the moment the sound of the recitations stopped, he would immediately come out. So, we were forced to adopt this "shouting policy," taking turns to shout out loud. The noisy chorus served as our smoke screen for playing around. Speaking of the sounds of recitations, it reminds me of the street performers from Jiangbei. When they perform their magic tricks on the stage, there are always gongs and drums to add to the atmosphere, creating a deafening racket that makes your head spin. The performers themselves raise their voices even higher, gesturing wildly and chanting incantations. The clamor creates opportunities for sleight of hand. Once the gongs and drums stop, everything is over.

Isn't Japan doing the same thing now? Before covertly deploying troops to occupy a certain place, they always fabricate some facts, rambling on and on about all sorts of things, leaving you completely baffled. By the time the international community tries to pay attention, "the rice has already been cooked," and the plan has become a reality.

As for China? After the September 18th Incident, slogans like "long-term resistance," "sleeping on brushwood and tasting gall," "quietly awaiting resolution from the League of Nations," "pacifying internally before resisting externally," etc., sound rather confusing to those of us unfamiliar with logic. However, whether they are also adopting this "shouting policy" without actually implementing it is something only those important figures who have spoken know in their hearts.

名譽黃金和美人

Fame, Gold, and Beauty

— 張芷痕

— Zhang Zhihen

丨幻滅的經過丨

丨The Process of Disillusionment丨

After several years of dedicated study in the New World, Mr. Yu obtained a doctorate in electrical engineering. Gilded with success, he returned to his homeland full of vigor. He wrote many papers, which were published in various prestigious journals, and his reputation gradually grew. Everyone in the national academic circle knew the great name of Dr. Yu Shifang.

The presidents of various universities expressed their admiration for Dr. Yu and vied to recruit him. Dr. Yu even held professorships at six universities simultaneously, traveling between ×××× several times a week. His monthly income, including writing fees, amounted to as much as eight or nine hundred yuan.

"Even heroes cannot escape the trap of beautiful women." The temptations of the typical New Era woman made Dr. Yu feel depressed and troubled, losing interest in life. Somehow, he formed a close friendship with Miss Huo, the most sought-after courtesan in ××.

From fame came gold, and from gold came beauty. Everything seemed to be a success.

×××××

Dr. Yu and Miss Huo's love was as sweet as honey. Cars, cinemas, upscale restaurants, dance halls – everything intoxicated them both. But the universities were waiting for Dr. Yu to lecture. No problem, he could ask friends to substitute. The monthly salary wasn't enough for Miss Huo's extravagant spending? No problem, he could borrow from friends.

The story of Dr. Yu's debauchery spread like wildfire. His friends no longer trusted him, and the university presidents no longer trusted him. He had borrowed all the money he could. As the second academic year began, no invitations from the universities arrived.

Dr. Yu's glory was not as bright as it once was, and his financial situation was dire. Miss Huo began to doubt him. Their honey-sweet love underwent a chemical reaction and turned as bland as water.

From beauty came the loss of fame, from the loss of fame came the loss of gold, and from the loss of fame and gold came the loss of beauty. Everything was shattered.

杜君竽遠自熱歸來與侯女士結婚詩以賀之

A Poem to Congratulate Mr. Du Yuyuan on Returning from Jehol and Marrying Ms. Hou

— 潘仰葊

— Pan Yang’an

何緣巧締同心結，

What fate wove your hearts together,

國難聲中佳耦成，

A fine couple formed amidst national crisis.

關外敵氛猶未靖，

Beyond the pass, the enemy's threat still lingers,

相期戒旦待鷄鳴。

Let us look forward to vigilance at dawn, awaiting the rooster's crow.

劍氣珠光映洞房，

The spirit of swords and the glimmer of pearls illuminate the bridal chamber,

征裝甫卸鬢凝霜，

Battle gear just removed, temples frosted with age.

枕邊共訴遼東根，

At the pillow, sharing tales of Liaodong roots,

不斬樓蘭恥不忘。

The shame of not slaying Loulan will never be forgotten.

願將蜜月先嘗膽，

Willing to first taste gall on this honeymoon,

肯把雄心付畫眉，

How could a noble aspiration be entrusted to mere adornment?

把臂共吟塞外曲，

Arm in arm, reciting songs of the frontier,

滿懷壯志兩相知。

Full of ambition, two souls understanding each other.

浸禮

Baptism

— 茸餘

— Rong Yu

A Western-style clock tower stands tall at the entrance; in the middle is a hall that can hold a thousand people, that is the well-known Christian church. Christianity is against the worship of idols, so one cannot find any decorations that represent God. A semi-circular pulpit is set up with a small table and a few chairs for the pastor's sermon. Below the platform lies a huge piano, surrounded by copper music stands for sheet music, as well as violins, clarinets, and copper drums; these are all for the choir. Beyond that are rows of benches, neatly arranged, for the listeners.

The large clock on the high tower, rings loudly; countless men, women, old and young, file into the church. Their solemn and pious appearances make you feel the wonders of religion. The old pastor on the platform has a kind face and an amiable attitude; his sincere tone truly represents the God of peace in heaven. Next is the hymn singing, beautiful string music accompanying the voices of the crowd: "Hallelujah, praise the Savior." It is like a group of angels singing. The old pastor closes his eyes and prays, the people below all stand together; they are also silent together, so quiet that almost everyone's breathing can be heard. "Amen" is said, and the congregation sits down.

The pastor begins to explain the reasons for the baptism, he says: "Jesus of the past also received baptism in the Jordan River. Now we believe in Jesus, so we must also be baptized, on the one hand to continue the work of Jesus; on the other hand to show that the old sins have been washed away, and new life has come again."

The believers being baptized, men and women, line up in front of the pastor. The pastor blesses them one by one. Then he tells them to separate into men's and women's changing rooms. At this time, the pool behind the platform is filled with warm water; the old pastor, wearing a sacred robe made of cowhide, stands in the water. The choir below is singing "Hallelujah, praise the Savior" in a melodious voice. The believers being baptized, one by one wearing single garments, stand in the water. The old pastor blesses them, one by one, they are immersed completely in the water, and then he helps them up, doing it in order. The baptism is over; the music has also stopped. The old pastor is exhausted; the baptized believers also seem to have taken a solemn cold bath.

長篇小說

Full-Length Novel

東北四連長

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— 張恨水

— Zhang Henshui

第二回陋室結芳鄰暗欽健叟權家擇良伴痛詆貧娃

Chapter Two: Humble Abode Forms Neighborly Relations, Secretly Admiring the Robust Old Man, Powerful Family Chooses a Good Match, Bitterly Denouncing the Poor Girl

Accumulating anger until his face turned red to the roots of his ears, Ji Zhi lowered his head and said, "She... she is also a good person..." Hou Zhi slammed his chopsticks and bowl down, placed both hands on the edge of the table, and looked at him, asking, "What good person? I must ask you to enlighten me, is she good because she runs around in the streets?" As he spoke, he turned to the old servant woman standing to the side and said, "In the future, if that poor girl comes, ignore her, just say whoever she's looking for isn't home." The old servant woman agreed. Hou Zhi was in such a rage that Mrs. Gan could only look at the two of them and smile. After a long while, she said, "There's no need to get so angry over this." She glanced at Hou Zhi, then smiled at Ji Zhi, saying, "Don't be impatient, if you want to find a wife, I can help you as your sister-in-law, I know people from all walks of life. That old maid, being from a poor family and lacking any modern knowledge, isn't a good match for you. Don't pay any attention to her." What else could Ji Zhi say? He could only quickly finish his meal and return to his own room. From afar, he could still hear his brother in the main room repeating "poor girl" over and over again. In his heart, he thought, "I didn't expect my brother to get so angry. Could it be that the Yang family has done something improper that he found out about?" To say that the old maid runs around in the streets is nothing important. First of all, that's how Manchu women are. Secondly, there are only a mother and daughter in her family, so either the mother or the daughter has to go out to buy things. There's nothing wrong with that. Even if the old maid has done something improper, well water doesn't interfere with river water, it has nothing to do with us. It's just that my brother said that if she comes in the future, we shouldn't pay attention to her. If she really comes and gets the cold shoulder, wouldn't she be embarrassed? The only thing to do is to tell her not to come anymore. But then again, how can I say such a thing to someone? Can I just plainly tell her, 'Don't come to my house anymore?' Doing it that way is worse than hitting her or scolding her. But if I don't say that, and she comes to the house and gets the cold shoulder, can I bear to let her suffer such a great loss? If that really happens, then we'll have to break off relations with each other." Ji Zhi thought and thought, but he couldn't come up with a solution. The incident hasn't even happened yet, and he's already in a dilemma. (23)

兒童的樂園

Children's Paradise

— 楚

— Chu

鶴與蝦

The Crane and the Shrimp

有一隻鶴，久住在池塘邊的樹上，那池塘裏生了許多魚蝦。鶴就靠魚蝦爲生的。後來鶴的年齡漸老，身體也不能行動，連魚也不能捕了，所以常常空腹飢餓，身體愈加瘦弱了。那鶴到了這時，想到：「年輕的時候，若是能夠多勞動，貯蓄了多少糧草自然不至有今日的樣子」心裏很懊悔過去的懶惰。某日，它在池塘邊彿徊，時時嘆息，忽然看見一隻蝦，那蝦問道：「鶴君，你爲什麽緣故，這樣頽喪呢？你不必呆想，趕緊去尋些東西吃吧，」鶴答道：「我的肚子，並不飢餓，我因爲想到今天早晨，有兩位漁夫到這裏來，有一位漁夫，想把這池塘的水車乾，還有一位漁夫主張想先把那邊的池塘的水車乾，大槪不久就要着手了。我聽到他們的話，一則很爲你魚蝦們憂慮，二則我也不能常常同你們在這裏爲友了，所以我的心裏很不安啊！」那蝦聽到這話，非常驚駭，就告訴那魚蝦們，那些可憐的魚蝦也很驚駭，立刻游泳到岸邊，請求那鶴想法子救它們的命，說道：「我們見了你，本來也是大仇敵，過去你戕殺我同胞們，不必再提起。不過古人有句話：窮鳥入懷，獵夫也不殺它的。現在情勢很緊，假使一旦漁夫來車乾這池塘的水，那末我們的生命都休了。我們若是都爲漁夫所捕，你豈忍心麽？所以應當爲我們想個法子，保全同胞的生命。」鶴答道：「我没有和漁夫對抗的能力，恐怕想不出來好的法子，不過漁夫去車乾那邊池塘的水，非一朝一夕的，須要幾個月工夫，我當盡力帶你們到别的池塘裏去吧。那魚蝦們一聽這話，都是非常喜歡，說道：「那末就請你帶我們去吧。」於是鶴就從這天起，開始搬魚蝦到他處去了。不料它每天早晨，　了二三尾的魚，飛到山上，把魚吃得乾乾凈凈。因此鶴的身體，也漸漸肥大，它以爲魚蝦們墮其彀中，從此都在它的掌中了。有一天，他照例的飛到池塘邊去　魚，看見有一隻大蝦等候。鶴就把蝦　到山上，那時這蝦看見地上有許多魚骨，知道以前鶴借代爲搬家爲名，都給它果腹了。它猛然的升開兩箝，箝住鶴的頭頸，鶴無法擺脫，一瞬之間，它的喉管被蝦箝斷，翻身死在地上。這時蝦雖不能在山上生活，然而已爲其他的魚蝦們報了大仇了。

There was a crane that lived for a long time on a tree by a pond. The pond was full of fish and shrimp. The crane relied on the fish and shrimp for food. Later, the crane grew old and could no longer move, so it could not catch fish, and was often hungry. Its body grew thinner. The crane thought at this point, "If I could have worked harder when I was young, I would have saved up a lot of food and would not be in this state today." It regretted its past laziness. One day, it paced back and forth by the pond, sighing from time to time. Suddenly, it saw a shrimp. The shrimp asked, "Mr. Crane, why are you so dispirited? Don't just stand there thinking. Go find something to eat." The crane replied, "My stomach isn't hungry. I was thinking that two fishermen came here this morning. One fisherman wanted to drain the pond, and the other advocated draining the pond over there first. They will probably start soon. When I heard their words, I was worried for you fish and shrimp, and also because I won't be able to be friends with you here for long. So, I am very uneasy!" When the shrimp heard this, it was very alarmed and told the other fish and shrimp. The poor fish and shrimp were also very alarmed and immediately swam to the shore and begged the crane to find a way to save their lives, saying, "When we see you, we are usually enemies. You have killed our fellow fish and shrimp in the past, but there is no need to mention that again. However, there is an old saying: 'A bird in distress, even a hunter will not kill it.' The situation is now very tight. If the fishermen come to drain the pond, then our lives will be over. If we are all caught by the fishermen, how can you bear it? Therefore, you should think of a way to save our fellow fish and shrimp." The crane replied, "I have no ability to confront the fishermen. I am afraid I can't think of a good way, but it will take months for the fishermen to drain the water from that pond. I will do my best to take you to another pond." When the fish and shrimp heard this, they were very happy and said, "Then please take us there." So, from that day on, the crane began to move the fish and shrimp to another place. Unexpectedly, every morning, it caught two or three fish, flew to the mountain, and ate the fish clean. Therefore, the crane's body gradually grew fatter. It thought that the fish and shrimp were in its grasp and that they were now all under its control. One day, as usual, it flew to the pond to catch fish, and saw a large shrimp waiting. The crane caught the shrimp and flew to the mountain. At that time, the shrimp saw many fish bones on the ground and knew that the crane was using the relocation as a pretext to fill its stomach. It suddenly opened its pincers and clamped the crane's neck. The crane could not get rid of it. In an instant, the crane's throat was cut off by the shrimp's pincers, and it fell to the ground and died. At this time, although the shrimp could not live on the mountain, it had avenged the great hatred for the other fish and shrimp.

五指何故不齊

Why Are the Five Fingers Not the Same Length?

人類的手，原來是爲走的作用，五個手指的長短不齊，就是爲支持重心的緣故。好比犬貓的趾爬行一般的，後來人體進化，漸漸的把原來的使用變更了。前脚（手）的爬行的效用，因代遠年深環境物質的關係，比後脚（足）愈加進步。後脚因爲專門用以走路的關係，慢慢的退化了。加以後脚的脚趾比前脚爲短，他的活動作用，當然要比前脚爲差啊。

The human hand was originally used for walking. The unequal length of the five fingers is for the sake of supporting the center of gravity. Like the toes of dogs and cats used for crawling, later, with human evolution, the original use gradually changed. The crawling function of the forelegs (hands), due to the distance of time and the environmental material, is more advanced than the hind legs (feet). Because the hind legs are specifically used for walking, they have slowly degenerated. In addition, the toes of the hind legs are shorter than those of the forelegs, so their active function is naturally worse than that of the forelegs.

洗浴時的注意

Precautions When Bathing

我們平常洗浴的水，温度應當在四十度内外，不可過于冷，也不可過于熱。普通有這温度，身上的黴菌，就能齣消滅了。所以當入浴的時候，先把全身浸熱水五分鐘，使身上的汚海與附着皮膚的黴菌，吸收熱水，那末再用絲爪經或粗布一擦，容易把身上的垢汚洗去。但是洗浴時，面部千萬不可洗，深恐身體上或浴缸裏的齷龊東西，傳染到限耳鼻口裏去。

The water we usually use for bathing should be around 40 degrees Celsius, not too cold or too hot. At this temperature, the mold on the body can be eliminated. Therefore, when entering the bath, first soak the whole body in hot water for five minutes, so that the dirt and mold attached to the skin absorb the hot water. Then, wipe with a silk sponge or coarse cloth to easily wash away the dirt from the body. However, do not wash the face during bathing, for fear that dirty things from the body or in the bathtub will infect the eyes, ears, nose, and mouth.

廠方不限價抛出

標粉跌勢甚猛

Flour Plummets Sharply As Mills Dump Unrestricted

Yesterday, the flour market did not show any significant fluctuations after the morning opening. As both Zihgam and Chicago wheat quotations fluctuated in different directions by about a dime, market participants remained composed. However, the flour market became increasingly sluggish and weak during the following trading sessions due to the continuous dumping of flour from Foo Foong, whose sales volume was quite large. Moreover, some merchants from Ke Pang continued dumping, the flour market became extremely bearish. The afternoon trading session saw a large collapse, as mills dumped remaining products irrespective of market prices. Consequently, the lock up which lasted for a half-month came to a conclusion. Amid heavy selling pressure, flour prices plummeted, and it was rumored that Niu Sze & Co. contracted to import 3,000 tons of wheat at a price as low as 3.324 yuan per ton. This rumor made the market participants very nervous, and caused prices to fall. The prices for May, June and July contracts declined to as low as 1.705 yuan. The price levels were close to the historical low. The market will become unimaginable if imported wheat price goes lower. As a result, the current month contract fell by two fen compared with yesterday, while the prices for April to July contracts each fell by three fen, and the August contract fell by three and a half fen.

忍痛出檔……小去二三分

Reluctantly Cutting Losses...Slight Losses of Two to Three Fen

Yesterday, the wheat futures market saw little price movement in the morning session, the sentiment was still negative because very few buyers showed up and the selling of flour was smooth. As a result, the price of wheat fell. Afternoon trading also experienced a collapse. It was difficult for the market to support the price as the price of flour plunged. Finally, because the dealers were ordering wheat continuously, the risk in keeping the stocks was too high, so most of them chose to cut their losses. The prices for futures contracts dropped steadily. As a result, the current month contract fell by two fen compared with yesterday, the April contract fell by three fen. The prices for May and June contracts had no price comparison, the July contract fell by four fen, and the August contract fell by seven fen.

Page 18

Free Talk

出賣靈魂的秘訣

The Secret to Selling One's Soul

— 何家幹

— By He Jiagan

幾年前，胡適博士曾經玩過一套。五鬼閙中華，的把戲，那是說：這世界上並無所謂帝國主義之類在侵略中國，倒是中國自己該着「貧窮」，「愚昧」…等五個鬼，鬧得大家不安寗。現在，胡適博士又發見了第六個鬼！呌做仇恨。這個鬼不但閙中華，而且禍延友邦，鬧到東京去了。因此，胡博士對症發藥，預備向「日本朋友」上條陳。

A few years ago, Dr. Hu Shih played a trick called "Five Ghosts Haunting China," which claimed that there was no such thing as imperialism invading China. Instead, China was plagued by five ghosts: "poverty," "ignorance," etc., causing unrest among the people. Now, Dr. Hu Shih has discovered a sixth ghost! It's called hatred. This ghost not only haunts China but also harms friendly nations, causing trouble in Tokyo. Therefore, Dr. Hu is prescribing a remedy, preparing to make recommendations to his "Japanese friends."

據博士說：「日本軍閥在中國暴行所造成之仇恨，到今日已頗難消除」，「而日本决不能用暴力征服中國」，（見報載胡適之最近談話，下同）。道是值得憂慮的：難道眞的没有方法征服中國嗎？不，法子是有的。「九世之仇，百年之友，均在覺悟不覺悟之關頭上，」！「日本只有一個方法可以征服中國，卽懸崖勒馬，澈底停止侵略中國，反過來征服中國民族的心。

According to the doctor, "The hatred caused by the atrocities of Japanese warlords in China is difficult to eliminate today," and "Japan can never conquer China by force." (See recent remarks by Hu Shih as reported in the newspapers, same below). This is a matter of concern: Is there really no way to conquer China? No, there is a way. "Enmity of nine generations and friendship of a hundred years depend on whether one is enlightened or not!" "Japan has only one way to conquer China: to rein in its horses at the precipice, completely stop invading China, and instead conquer the hearts of the Chinese people."

這據說是「征服中國的唯一方法。」不錯，古代的儒敎軍師，，總說「以德服人者王，其心誠服也」。胡適博士不愧爲日本帝國主義的軍師。但是，從中國小百姓方面說來，這却是出賣靈魂的唯一秘訣。中國小百姓實在「愚昧」，原不懂得自己的民族性」，所以他們一向會仇恨。如果日本陛下大發慈悲，居然採用胡博士的條陳，那末，所謂「忠孝仁愛信義和平」的中國固有文化，就可以恢復：！因爲日本不用暴力而用軟功的王道，中國民族就不至於再生仇恨，因爲没有仇恨，自然更不抵抗，因爲更不抵抗，自然就更和平，更忠孝……中國的肉體固然買到了，中國的靈魂也被征服了。

This is said to be "the only way to conquer China." Indeed, ancient Confucian military strategists always said, "He who conquers with virtue reigns, and his heart is truly conquered." Dr. Hu Shih is indeed a military strategist for Japanese imperialism. However, from the perspective of ordinary Chinese people, this is the only secret to selling one's soul. Ordinary Chinese people are indeed "ignorant" and do not understand their own national character," so they have always harbored hatred. If His Majesty the Emperor of Japan, in his great mercy, were to adopt Dr. Hu's recommendations, then the inherent Chinese culture of "loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, trustworthiness, righteousness, and peace" could be restored! Because Japan would not use violence but instead use the gentle power of the kingly way, the Chinese people would not generate hatred again. Because there would be no hatred, they would naturally not resist. Because they would not resist, there would naturally be more peace and more loyalty and filial piety... China's body would indeed be bought, and China's soul would also be conquered.

可惜的是這「唯一方法」的實行，完全要　日本陛下的覺悟。如果不覺悟，那又怎麽辦？胡博士回答道：「到無可奈何之時，眞的接受一種恥辱的城下之盟」好了。那眞是無可奈何的呵丨因爲那時候「仇恨鬼」是不肯走的，這始終是中國民族性的汚點，卽爲日本計，也非萬全之道。

Unfortunately, the implementation of this "only method" completely depends on the enlightenment of His Majesty the Emperor of Japan. If he is not enlightened, then what can be done? Dr. Hu replied, "When there is no other option, we must truly accept a humiliating treaty of surrender." That would truly be helpless! Because at that time, the "ghost of hatred" would not leave, and this would always be a stain on the Chinese national character. Even for Japan's sake, it is not a perfect solution.

因此，胡博士準備出席太平洋會議，再去「忠告」一次他的日本朋友：征服中國並不是没有法子的，請接受我們出賣的靈魂罷，何况這並不難，所謂澈底停止侵略」，原只要執行「公平的」李頓報告，丨仇恨自然就銷除了！

Therefore, Dr. Hu is preparing to attend the Pacific Conference to give his Japanese friends another "sincere piece of advice": There is indeed a way to conquer China. Please accept our souls that we are selling. Moreover, it is not difficult. The so-called "completely stopping aggression" only requires implementing the "fair" Lytton Report, and hatred will naturally be eliminated!

North Sichuan Road

— Ma Guoliang

New Year's red lanterns, Bank of China, Tang Bailin, large white dishes, cars, people in red and green, fish congee and minced pork noodles, Moon Palace Dance Hall, Hengchang Tailor Shop, renovated in 1933, the most reasonable prices, Xinya Tea Room, Shanghai Grand Theatre, Secrets of the English Court… one of the world's top ten films…

The upper section of North Sichuan Road is still so lively, a chaotic mass of people fills the street. But just past the Shanghai Grand Theatre, it becomes so quiet and dark, as if the people and cars above… once they get here, they're like ghosts who've covered their eyes, everyone turns their heads and no longer runs downwards; suddenly, the bottom becomes so calm.

Fortunately, my eyes haven't been covered by ghosts, I can still see the road ahead, so I keep running into the darkness.

Two or three empty rickshaws are slowly pulled along sluggishly. Under the dim light, as if recognizing someone walking, the empty vehicles desperately rush forward as if in a race, the oiled canvas hoods making flapping sounds.

To the right of the standard clock, on the wasteland that was leveled by the January 28th artillery fire, several young children are squatting amidst the rubble. They’ve probably just finished selling the evening newspapers and are putting on a practiced, adult-like appearance as they smoke and argue about something…

How strange! My heart skipped a beat! Aren’t these the children from the movie "A Way to Live" turned into real living people, jumping out of the screen! But then I mocked my own foolishness, the children in "A Way to Live" had already run to the factory and completed a section of railway! Only our children have the fortune to run around randomly, with no one caring or paying attention, smoking if they want to smoke!

The wonton seller walks around at the entrance of Dade Lane, hitting the bamboo clapper in his hand, shouting, "Wonton noodles!" Stretching his neck, he looks up at the people living upstairs. But the upper floors are dark and silent. Nothing can be conjured out of thin air. There's still no movement from above. Pshaw! The wonton seller blows his nose, "Wonton noodles!" The bamboo clapper clatters, the sound vibrating in the quiet street center, making people shiver!

Three Japanese soldiers, thoroughly imitating the drunken steps of Americans, stagger and stumble from behind, brushing past me. Passing the entrance of a small eatery, one of them pushes over the wooden sign placed at the doorway, and then they brag and walk on. This is the so-called spirit of Bushido of the Yamato race, I thought.

The heavy footsteps gradually disappear ahead of me, and Baoxing Road is left behind. The mud in the pool under Yokohama Bridge reflects the desolate moonlight above. It's even colder and lonelier. People are all asleep, aren't they? Yes, they've been fast asleep for a long time. But there will always be a tomorrow when they wake up, a day when they finally jump up.

The tall building of the Japanese Elementary School, like an arrogant giant, stands coldly by the roadside. The roar of January 28th didn't shatter it, but in the future, it won't be able to escape an even greater roar, I thought, as my legs continued to move forward. It's even quieter now! Like a tomb—it really is a tomb! On the morning of the second day of January 28th, I crawled out of this tomb, passing through many bloody bayonets, escaping with my life!

Walking further down, I felt even more isolated. Suddenly recalling the splendor of the upper section of North Sichuan Road, I couldn’t quite believe my eyes just now. I immediately turned around and ran back, running to the entrance of the Shanghai Grand Theatre in one breath. Instantly, everything brightened up, and the people and cars were still such a chaotic mess, New Year's red lanterns, people in red and green... Tang Bailin...

I turned my head again and ran back, and in front of me was still such a desolate scene, and darkness! Believe it or not, anyway, I haven't grown another pair of eyes on my head.

Over there is money, extravagance, laughter, pleasure, pleasure, and more pleasure; here is a scene of desolation, a scene of darkness, mixed with painful sighs. Look, friend, never mind anything else, just one North Sichuan Road has two worlds!

The laughter over there doesn't reach here, and the sighs here can't be heard over there either.

Wait and see, I thought. No longer having the strength to walk out, I turned into my apartment hidden in the darkness.

Terrifying darkness! I leaned my head out of the window and looked around, sticking out my tongue. But when I jumped into bed, I immediately comforted myself:

People living next to a volcano won't be there forever; when the sun comes out tomorrow, it will light up here too!

Elegant Person

— Zhang Tianyi

It is said that people are divided into elegant and vulgar, and that everything has old and new distinctions, so there are old elegant people and new elegant people. Old elegant people recite five-character and seven-character lines about wind, flowers, snow, and moon, play the seven-stringed zither, frolic with women, play with antique calligraphy and paintings, or even smoke opium, and so on. New elegant people, on the other hand, exert effort on nightingales and roses, write lines of poetry, paint oil paintings, play the Western pipa, lie on their "lover's" lap and practice their singing voice, or take a nap like that, and so on. There are many varieties, too numerous to record.

Although the styles of new and old elegant people are different, the conditions for being elegant are the same. Elegant people must be scholars, knowing more than ordinary people. If you don’t have money to pay for tuition and uniform fees (in many schools, students who don’t pay for uniforms are expelled), you can forget about becoming an elegant person. Secondly, they must be detached from the mundane world. It is said that elegant people "do not engage in production," and don't care about the bustling and troublesome affairs of the world, and despise discussing fiery political matters.

However, it is truly strange: the vulgar things that elegant people do are much more sophisticated than those of vulgar people. Our ancient elegant people all mixed well with high officials and nobles. Even the immortal who was so elegant that he seemed to have no earthly desires had to fawn over the wealthy and serve as a "court attendant" in the palace, amusing the emperor. As for someone like Mr. Tao, who didn't care for five pecks of rice and "returned," he was an exception, but that was because he had "fields" to "return" to.

This is talking about the old elegant people.

As for the new elegant people, apart from a few new-style "court attendants," the rest are all "born at an unfortunate time": they have no "soulmates." Because there are too many "new figures" now. No one appreciates them. Then "return," but the countryside is plagued by natural disasters and human calamities year after year, and there are no "fields" to "return" to. And what's worse, imperialism is constantly bombing us with cannons and dropping bombs, and everyone is about to fight them to the death. This is a vulgar matter, but it is a matter of life and death. If you are not careful, even your elegant life is hard to guarantee.

So what to do? There are a few paths:

One, be elegant in a way that is half old and half new, in order to find "soulmates."

Two, just sigh and do nothing else.

Three, come up with a new theory of national salvation. Because staying in an ivory tower and making art more sophisticated can also bring glory to the country.

Except for the second option, which is slightly passive, the other two are both maintaining the identity of an elegant person and being practical, which is very appropriate.

Random Words from Qu Lu

— Zi Zhan

(Ten) (One) Essay Formula

Recently, I saw an article by Mr. Yu Dafu in the "Free Talk" section about the essay formula, which reminded me of an interesting incident when I first took up the teaching post seventeen years ago. I once said that scholars today have nothing to do, so they descend to teach, and if they have no expertise in teaching, they descend to teach Chinese literature. If we borrow the constant saying of my old friend Mr. Li Wu, the so-called mentally challenged, Chinese literature teachers belong to this group, without a doubt, and I am one of them. When I was young, I dabbled in writing and was ranked alongside teachers and Confucian scholars, holding a book and stepping onto the podium, feeling invincible. However, I was the youngest, and my colleagues often looked down on me because of this. After I read the students' papers twice, I discovered an essay formula used by the whole class:

"Living in the world… why? Because… from this perspective… wouldn't it be… ah… alas…"

Let's take the so-called revolution of today as the topic and apply the formula:

"Living in the world, one must engage in revolution, why? Because if a person engages in revolution, in a small way, it is easy to find a job and eat, and in a big way, it is not difficult to be promoted and become wealthy. But the so-called revolution today is a matter of moderation; not leaning to one side is called moderation, and not being extreme is called gentleness. Moderation is the highest virtue! Therefore, being too revolutionary is degeneration, inevitably leading to murder and arson. Being too unrevolutionary is corruption, inevitably leading to senility and incompetence. Achieving the middle ground is revolution; once one is revolutionary, one is a comrade; if a comrade is most loyal, one can become a great person. From this perspective, of all the people today, none are better than revolutionaries. If one wants to make one's revolution great, how can one not first be loyal to one's so-called loyalty? Alas, this is why there are more and more loyal comrades, and why the revolution is successful."

In short, any topic can be put into this formula. At that time, I jokingly made a banner and a couplet and posted them on the door:

Alas

Living in the world why because

From this perspective wouldn't it be ah

And I warned the students: anyone who commits these sixteen characters in their essays will be penalized by having to rewrite them, and those who commit them again must slap their own palms. The whole school was in an uproar, and I almost left to avoid the situation. Finally, two or three old classmates interceded for me, and I was spared being ostracized. But in the end, the students warned each other not to use this essay formula again.

Long Fiction

The Crossroads of the Times and Love

— Zhang Guanping

"But that is impossible. It insults women, and it is also a sign of..."

He decided to leave. Because Madam Cao's demonstration was really too intense. He wanted to get up several times, but he felt that his legs below were just limp and couldn't stand up. He still stole another hungry glance at Madam Cao's pinkish-white chest.

He knew that he was standing at a crossroads. He couldn't give up the nobility and purity like Peizhu. But at the same time, he felt that the only way to cure his current feelings of loneliness was to seek some unthinkable comfort from women like Madam Hezi.

"What do you have to say to Shiguang? ...I know, you're all no good! You two must have made a secret agreement beforehand, and now you're trying to drag me along! Mr. Lin, Acao already likes playing that game enough, and you're trying to drag him out to play again, I really can't agree to it! ...Men and women are equal! If a man can leave his wife and find another mistress outside, then a wife can also move freely! Mr. Lin, do you think that's right?"

Madam Cao's words were like a wave that hadn't settled down, and then a surprising peak rose again. So he couldn't help but argue with her for a while. When the argument couldn't be resolved, he suddenly heard a sound on the stairs, a series of thumping sounds.

"Old Lin, you're here? What kind of wind blew you here?"

They had another long argument about the issue of gender equality, and before they knew it, it was past one o'clock. Because Haiquan helped Cao Shiguang and Madam Cao argue, she said she would punish him by making him treat them to dinner. Haiquan naturally agreed. Hearing Haiquan agree to her request, she was as happy as a child again, hurrying to apply makeup and change clothes.

Twenty-nine

Qiuying was very happy when she heard that Haiquan had asked Shiguang to find a garret, wanting to move over and live in the same alley with them.

"Mr. Lin, wait a few more days. The garret there is about to become available. Isn't the New Year's holiday coming soon? The student living in the garret is going home, and he has already returned the room to the second landlord. The second landlord has also asked me to introduce someone familiar to him. It's only seven dollars, including electricity, incredibly cheap."

Shao Yuan-chong Receives Foreign Correspondents

Reporting on Our Country's Unified Determination to Resist Japan

Striving for National Survival with a Spirit of Fearlessness

Hoping Friendly Nations Understand and Provide Moral Support in Friendship

(Beiping) Shao Yuan-chong hosted foreign journalists at the German Hotel on the 25th and delivered the following speech: Gentlemen, it is a great pleasure to meet with you all today. You have all been engaged in journalism in China for many years and have provided much support for Chinese friendship. You are all good friends of China. China is currently in an unfortunate situation. The Chinese people are willing to exert their own efforts to overcome this national crisis, and they hope that you will provide moral assistance to convey the truth of the Chinese Kuomintang's struggle to all countries of the world, so that they will not be blinded by biased news. This would be of great help to China. Since the founding of the Republic of China, progress has often been hindered by unexpected obstacles, so that political construction, economic construction, and cultural construction have not yet achieved the expected results. However, we must not be disappointed because China, with its land, population, and history, cannot easily completely reform old habits and create a new foundation in a short period of time. Ten or twenty years is a very short time in history, so we must not be disappointed by the failure to completely succeed in reform. We must only work harder to achieve construction success, and we firmly believe that continuous efforts and a determination to persevere will enable us to achieve final success and create a glorious new life for the Chinese nation and state. The reasons for the obstacles to China's past construction progress are numerous, but the biggest reason is the instigation, destruction, aggression, and oppression of Japanese imperialism. Therefore, since the Qing Dynasty and the Yuan Shikai era, all movements for innovation and efforts to build the country by the Chinese people have been constantly subjected to direct or indirect oppression and destruction by Japanese imperialism, either by supporting old forces to suppress new forces, or by using anti-democratic forces to confront democratic forces. This historical fact of the past few decades can be illustrated by any example. Since the Meiji era, the only national strategy of Japanese imperialism has been to annex the Asian continent, threaten the world, and create the world's sole military power. China's natural resources are inexhaustible. After annexing Korea as the first step, Japan proceeded to annex China's Northeast, and then to annex the whole of China. With its barbaric military force and China's infinite resources, it would have no fear of being an enemy to all the powerful countries in the world. Therefore, the frequent and blatant serious oppression of China by Japanese imperialism in recent years is actually a challenge to the whole world, and China is the first to be sacrificed. However, the Chinese nation has never failed to encounter serious foreign insults in its more than four thousand years of history. However, the Chinese nation, with its perseverance and continuous efforts, has eventually been able to drive out foreign races or assimilate them. It will never be oppressed by foreign races for long. The Chinese nation is inherently peaceful, but within peace, it has a strong spirit, that is, to be able to save itself, love its national history, and worship heroes who sacrifice for the nation. For example, Yue Fei, who struggled throughout his life to defend his country, is consistently worshiped by the Chinese, old and young, as a national hero. His spirit is deeply rooted in the psychology of the general public. This is the inner expression of the Chinese national spirit. Therefore, no matter what the era, the Chinese nation has been able to resist foreign enemies, which is the expression of this national spirit. This national spirit is what sustains the life of the Chinese nation in the past, present, and future. Although the Chinese nation is now under serious oppression by Japanese imperialism, we firmly believe that our persevering struggle will be able to break through the serious environment with our own efforts and the encouragement of international justice, and give a powerful lesson to the violent invaders, so that they will suffer their own evil retribution. We are fighting with a spirit of fearlessness, so even if our material equipment is not as good as others, we can still use ancient weapons, such as broadswords, to fight against modern aircraft and cannons. We can make the entire nation sacrifice to resist oppressive forces, but we cannot allow ourselves to be subdued by unreasonable oppression. There is an ancient Chinese saying, "Better to be a shattered jade than a whole tile." This is what we use to encourage ourselves. This is what we use to encourage our struggle. John Hay of the United States said, "The center of the world's future problems is in the Pacific, and the center of the Pacific problems is in China." Sun Yat-sen also said, "China's peace is the foundation of world peace, and the success of the Chinese revolution is the guarantee of world peace." Therefore, the problem of China is actually the problem of the world, and the oppression and aggression of China by any power is a crisis for world peace. Therefore, the struggle of the Chinese nation is not only for the survival of its own nation, but also for the protection of world peace. The Chinese nation can cooperate in friendship with all nations of the world, and the Chinese state can cooperate in friendship with all countries of the world. China is happy to work together with the international community on all economic and cultural undertakings that can increase the common interests and development of China and the world, and to complete them together in accordance with Sun Yat-sen's principles of economic construction. However, if anyone wants to use military aggression and oppression to separate China's land and people and infringe upon China's sovereignty, then the Chinese people will continue to develop their spirit of resistance and fight for their nation and sovereignty. Because the Chinese nation is fighting for the nation, even if there is only one person left, he will fight to his last breath. This is the unanimous determination of China at this time, and it is also the common policy of the Chinese government and people today, which cannot be changed, nor can anyone change it. I am very happy to be able to meet with you all today, and I hope to have opportunities to shake hands in the future. I would like to express the general opinion of the Chinese people in a brief speech, and I hope that you will spread this opinion to the general public of friendly countries, so that they can understand the direction of the Chinese people's efforts and provide moral support in friendship. I would also like to ask you all to raise a glass and wish you good health. (Central News Agency dispatch, morning of the 26th)

| Issues Statement |

Chiang, Feng, and Yan Share Anti-Japanese Determination

(Nanjing) Li Liejun arrived in Nanjing at 8:00 AM on the 26th. After staying for two or three days, he will go to Shanghai to attend an important central meeting on the 27th, and will also make suggestions. Li issued the following statement:

French Cabinet Discusses

Four-Power Cooperation Plan

Temporarily Does Not Decide on Attitude

Reuters, Paris, 25th: The French Cabinet today discussed the four-power understanding plan drafted by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini for France, Britain, Germany, and Italy. It lasted a long time. According to a semi-official communiqué, the Cabinet will not make a decision for the time being, but will wait to ascertain the attitudes of the governments concerned, especially those that have not been consulted before, and then decide how to proceed. The Cabinet also discussed the overdue payment of war debts to the United States.

The Little Entente

Is a Force Not to Be Scorned

Communiqué Issued After Opening of Regular Meeting in Geneva

Opposes Any Agreement That Impedes Peace

Havas, Geneva, 25th: The Standing Committee of the Little Entente countries met in Geneva today and issued a communiqué stating, "The Standing Committee of the Little Entente countries, after carefully considering recent international events, believes that it is appropriate for countries to aspire to establish relations with each other and to resolve issues related to specific countries through cooperation. This cooperation can produce good results. However, if countries sign various treaties that force the signatory countries to take concrete decisions, or only allow the signatory countries to exert pressure on countries outside the treaty to achieve their goal of disposing of the rights of third countries, such means cannot be recognized by the Little Entente countries as conducive to good relations between countries. From a legal point of view, the property of others cannot be disposed of, directly or indirectly. Therefore, the Little Entente countries specifically reserve their rights regarding the desire of countries to conclude such treaties that infringe upon the rights and politics of the Little Entente countries. Such treaties have become a thing of the past and cannot exist after the establishment of the League of Nations. Moreover, there have been signs of proposals to amend treaties in recent negotiations, which is most regrettable. Mutual trust must be sought first if countries cooperate. The act of amending treaties cannot reassure countries or increase their trust. The result is only to provoke resolute resistance. For the sake of international peace, the Little Entente countries believe that all countries should pay attention to this. For this reason, the Little Entente countries believe that the powers of the respective countries should be concentrated and devoted to the work of building peace. There is no other way to maintain world peace and security."

Britain's

Position Gradually Consolidated

Optimistic Words from Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain

Reuters, London, 25th: Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain spoke optimistically about Britain's future in Birmingham last night, asking the people to trust the government so that the government could complete its work, saying that Britain's credit system has now been fully restored. People from other countries are now flocking to England, believing England to be a safer place. Britain, which had fallen to the world's third-largest exporter, has now regained its position as the world's first-largest exporter. More than two hundred new factories in Britain have been established with foreign investment, and no fewer than twenty foreign governments have asked to negotiate new commercial treaties with Britain. British agriculture has now been thoroughly reorganized, and farmers currently have greater hope and confidence in the future. As for the problem of the new Indian political system, it is very difficult. The government is well aware of the dangers, but it can eventually solve this problem by approaching it with patience, goodwill, wisdom, and perseverance. In the past week, the European situation has undergone great changes as a result of the British Prime Minister's visit to Geneva and Rome. The interests of British strategy have always been in maintaining peace, but it is not entirely true to say that we do not want to fight. In fact, what we want is a step further than fighting, to do our best to mediate and relieve other countries from the scourge of war. This is our responsibility.

There Is Talk of Revising and

Redistributing Mandated Territories

According to the Tokyo Jiji Shinpo, on the 20th, the London newspapers, regarding the meeting between British Prime Minister MacDonald and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, used Mussolini's peace treaty proposal as the theme, writing extensively about the content of the meeting and adding various explanations. Among them, the Conservative Party-related newspapers published a theory of redistributing mandated territories, the gist of which was "Mussolini agreed to MacDonald's disarmament proposal on the condition that the mandated territories of the League of Nations be revised and redistributed. For example, some of the small territories currently under British mandate will be ceded to Italy. Italy's supply of necessary raw materials will be increased from these regions. " (According to Japanese reports, after Britain released the news of the redistribution, it was extremely panicked, fearing that the South Pacific mandated territories would also be distributed to other countries.)

Closing Ceremony of the Japanese Diet

Fifty-One Government Bills Passed

Saito's Fate Hinges on Meeting with Prince Saionji

Dentsu, Tokyo, 26th: The 64th Diet concluded uneventfully yesterday. The closing ceremony was held in the House of Peers at 11:00 AM today. According to the Imperial Household Ordinance, the Emperor did not have to attend in person. Prime Minister Saito and other cabinet members, the speakers and vice-speakers of both houses, and Diet members successively entered the House from 9:00 AM, forgetting the political battles of yesterday and gathering together in joy. The bell rang at 10:00 AM to open the meeting. Prime Minister Saito proceeded to the throne, performed the most respectful bow, and received the Imperial Edict held by the Chief Cabinet Secretary. Amidst the most respectful bows of the officials, he held it and read it aloud. Speaker Tokugawa received the Imperial Edict, completed the ceremony, and withdrew.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 26th: After the Diet ended yesterday, Prime Minister Saito told reporters that he was very pleased that the Diet had closed uneventfully. He will pay full attention to the implementation of the budget. In the future, he will concentrate on reorganizing the tax system, financial reform, and administrative legal bills. Of the 53 bills submitted by the government, 51 were passed by both houses, and only two were not deliberated. The government must work harder on the diplomatic issues, ideological issues, and financial issues after withdrawing from the League of Nations. There are many domestic and foreign affairs now, and we are still in an extraordinary situation. The government can only be more aware of its increased efforts.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 26th: Now that the 64th Diet has ended, if the Saito Cabinet violates the expectations of the Seiyukai and maintains its government, the Seiyukai's anti-government attitude will inevitably increase. Although Prime Minister Saito said at the closing of the Diet that he had not yet left the extraordinary situation and would continue to take responsibility in the future, it is doubtful whether the current cabinet, which includes Seiyukai cabinet members, can proceed smoothly without problems of disunity. The issue of responsibility for Justice Minister Oyama and Education Minister Hatoyama cannot be ignored. In short, Prime Minister Saito's visit to Prince Saionji on the 6th or 7th will truly determine the direction of the current government.

World Astronomers

Gather on Uninhabited Islands in the South Pacific

to Observe the Solar Eclipse

Nichi-Ren, Tokyo, 26th: Famous astronomers from around the world will gather on an uninhabited island in the South Pacific to observe the total solar eclipse and study important issues in astrophysics. Japan has decided to send Dr. Saotome of the Tokyo Observatory and Dr. Yamaki of the Kyoto Kasan Observatory to participate in the research. The uninhabited island is an isolated island in the open sea, with many reefs nearby, making it difficult to navigate. Ordinary ships cannot go there. The Japanese Navy authorities, in order to assist this valuable academic research, have dispatched the warship Komahashi to escort the group.

World League Against Anti-Semitism

Announces Boycott of German Goods

Unless the Tyranny Worsens, the Holy See Wishes to Intervene

Political Prisoners in German Prisons Are Not Being Tortured

Reuters, London, 25th: The World League Against Anti-Semitism, which had previously announced a boycott of German goods, today re-announced the boycott and extended it to German-owned restaurants and cinemas showing German films, expressing its protest against Germany's treatment of Jews. Rumors that the Pope in Rome would intervene have been denied. According to a Reuters correspondent in the Holy City today, there will be no diplomatic action unless the tyranny worsens. German Reichstag President Göring today told a foreign press correspondent in Berlin that the German government does not want to discriminate against Jews or interfere with their personal freedom. Göring also denied allegations of atrocities and murder, but admitted that there had been "isolated acts" in several cases, but that the government was now making every effort to prevent them from happening again. Foreign news correspondents were allowed by the German authorities to visit the prisons and speak freely with the political prisoners, who were rumored to be tortured or executed in prison. Communist leaders Thälmann and Torgler were among those detained. The Reuters correspondent met them at the police headquarters. Thälmann said that he was not suffering and had not been insulted. The others were the same. However, the author of "War," Lenn, criticized the food, accommodation, and general treatment in prison harshly. According to a senior police officer, there are currently 5,000 to 6,000 political prisoners in detention in Germany, and many of them have asked to be detained to avoid accidents. Since the government decided that Jews would no longer be allowed to serve as judges in German courts in Berlin from April 1, the Bavarian Minister of Justice has ordered that Jewish judges should not preside in criminal or admonition courts in the future, and Jewish prosecutors should not be allowed to serve as state lawyers.

Havas, Paris, 25th: A temporary committee has now been established in France to provide relief to Jews who are being treated unfairly in Germany. Former Prime Minister Painlevé and the Chief Rabbi of France are among the members.
