Reconciles with Key Party Figures

Havas, Berlin, 25th: It seems that Prime Minister Hitler and former key figure of the National Socialist Party Strasser will be reconciled. During General Schleicher's tenure as Federal Chancellor last December, Strasser strongly advocated cooperation between the National Socialist Party and the Schleicher cabinet. Hitler did not approve, and the two became estranged. As a result, Strasser was also dismissed. Since then, Strasser has not engaged in political activities.

American Labor Party Organs Oppose Wage Issues

Reuters, Washington, 26th: The Labor Committees of the Senate and House of Representatives today discussed President Roosevelt's plan to organize 250,000 people to undertake afforestation work to accommodate the unemployed. American Federation of Labor President Green delivered a speech today, attacking the method of hindering wage standards in peacetime labor groups. | Implementation Delayed |

Reuters, The Hague, 25th: The Dutch Colonial Department announced that the plan to restrict tea production in Dutch territories has been postponed from April 1. However, if tea growers in India and Ceylon implement the same plan, the Dutch East Indies may also implement it from April 15.

The Extremely Sharpened Conflict Between France and Italy, Paris Correspondence (February 25th)

Mussolini Implements a Counterattack

The Little Entente's Solidarity is Strengthened

People Severely Warn of the Danger of War

The conflict between the allied nations within France's sphere of influence and the fascist nations of Italy, Hungary, and Germany is continuously intensifying day by day. The focal point of the conflict, as before, lies on one hand in the arbitrary denial of the "Fascist Triangular Alliance," and on the other hand in the firm affirmation of the existence of the "Fascist Triangular Alliance." Mussolini vehemently declared in a cabinet meeting, "The news regarding the conclusion of an Italian-Hungarian-German alliance is simply unfounded. If the Foreign Affairs Committee did not mention this matter, then there would be no need to deny such news." At the same time, Mussolini published an essay, noting that it was written in Rome so that everyone would know who the author was. In this essay, Mussolini attacked France with unprecedented severity, saying that France's utterly excessive attempt to spread rumors is tantamount to openly disrupting peace. France spreads this poisonous atmosphere, causing confusion and unrest among the people of Europe. Who would still believe that France truly cherishes peace? In reality, France refuses to disarm, but in order to deceive others, it deliberately constructs secret alliances and castles in the air about war disasters on the banks of the Rhine and the Alps. No one has threatened France; only France, with its excessively enlarged military equipment, its selfishness, its complete ignorance of the needs of other nations, its allies, and its newspapers bought by the military industry, threatens Europe and the world.

This essay is like adding fuel to the fire. This challenging tone will naturally cause the expected reaction in France, but it has also aroused many comments in Germany. General Stohnegel's fascist newspaper, the "Berliner," seems like a schoolboy, very happy to see his brother scolding people so happily.

"Here, at least in a semi-official statement, France is exposed as the destroyer of peace, a great conspirator, and a cruel politician. The tone used in Mussolini's essay is the sharpest ever. Since the war, no such harsh tone has been used between European countries, not even by the former Allies. Due to the current vigorous instigation by France, a stormy mood is enveloping Rome and Paris. Mussolini's words are a manifestation of this stormy mood."

Indeed, these words are a manifestation of a stormy mood, and the so-called storm is the future new world war. Now, it is not just issuing declarations of war; the actual actions are enough to expose the severity of the danger of war, and they are everywhere.

Among France's protectorates, the solidarity of the "Little Entente" countries is further strengthened. Romania, Yugoslavia, and Czechoslovakia must act together and establish a joint "Permanent Committee" for leadership. Undoubtedly, this new treaty has political significance. It is naturally aimed at opposing the Italian-Hungarian-German attempt to change the European sphere of influence. The "Berliner" wrote about this,

"Yesterday's news about the close solidarity of the Little Entente will similarly affect the progress of European politics. This solidarity is clearly against Italy, Hungary, and Germany. This solidarity is France's last attempt. France only wants to reunite Czechoslovakia with Romania, which is already economically and financially bankrupt, and Yugoslavia, which is threatened by internal turmoil, to make them guardians of Versailles and "Trianon" (also in Versailles, the site of the 1919 treaty between Hungary and the Allies)."

In Belgrade (the capital of Yugoslavia) and Bucharest (the capital of Romania), the arrival of war is being calculated very seriously. A Vienna correspondent for a certain newspaper said, "...The mood in southeastern Europe is deteriorating day by day. People believe that the arrival of war seems like it is tomorrow."

The mood in Warsaw (the capital of Poland) is the same. Recent debates in parliament clearly show that the government party, from the Social Democrats and fake opposition parties all the way to the right wing, are all exhibiting a mood for war.

In recent weeks, France's influence has undoubtedly greatly expanded. Because Poland fears German invasion and Yugoslavia fears Italian invasion, the French government has taken advantage of this opportunity to consolidate the already unreliable "Godingen-Salonika route."

The French government has not shown any surprising skill in this effort. The victories the French government has achieved are almost unearned.

In many challenging speeches and essays north and south of the Alps, the question is often repeatedly asked, under whose help are these governments built, or are they under British help? The British government's attitude at the disarmament conference is a warning. The British [blank space] Eden's proposal to add a new clause to the Cairo Convention (that no conflict should be resolved by force under any circumstances) is just an attempt to temporarily delay the conference. The Frankfurter Zeitung (February 16th) published a London dispatch, pointing out that Britain does not believe that France is in danger of war, in order to later reach the following conclusion,

"When the British government was reorganized recently, some people in London wished that German foreign policy would not change. An interview in the Sunday Express completely shattered this illusion. In addition, anyone who pays attention to politics must point out that Germany has surprisingly lost its foundation in British political circles as a result of the new government's change in domestic strategy."

Since the German Fascists cannot get help from Britain, can they get help from the Soviet Union? Fascist government newspapers like the Berliner are vigorously promoting that the Hitler government's anti-communist domestic policy will absolutely not affect relations with the Soviet Union. The Frankfurter Zeitung (February 14th), on the other hand, contradicts this. It is very worried and affirms that France is constantly striving to establish closer relations between France and the Soviet Union.

"Of course, it cannot be said that the French government directly intends to conclude a military alliance with the Soviet Union, but the French government is working hard to stabilize the East, and in certain circumstances, it would not hesitate to conclude a certain military agreement. The Soviet Union's position is advancing every hour. If Germany and the Soviet Union had relations before, then it can now be said that these relations have completely disappeared. The Prime Minister's goal of defeating communism greatly helps France's efforts to win over the Soviet Union. This is natural."

The Frankfurter Zeitung has been carrying out a campaign against the danger of war for a week. This is the demand of a part of the German bourgeoisie. This part of the bourgeoisie is very afraid that the imperialist bourgeoisie's adventurous war will put German capitalism in greater danger than in 1918. The newspaper points out the danger of war and repeatedly declares, "Here (Paris), according to the existing signs, people are severely warning of the danger of war. This is terrible, but it must be said."

Yes, there is a danger of war in Paris, Marseille, Prague, Belgrade, Bucharest, as well as Rome, Budapest, and Berlin, and the danger of war is growing day by day.

Guangdong Province Decides to Complete the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan Railway

The Lechang to Luojiadu Section Will Be Constructed Immediately

The Construction Funds of 7 Million Yuan Have Also Been Raised

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section of the Yuehan Railway was previously planned by the Guangzhou-Shaoguan Railway Bureau, intending to allocate two-thirds of the Boxer Indemnity to construction costs, and also planning to issue 40 million yuan of Zhuzhou-Shaoguan public bonds starting from March of this year. Later, due to the increasing national crisis, the Ministry of Finance temporarily suspended the allocation of the indemnity, and the construction plan was hit. Li Xiangen, Director of the Guangzhou-Shaoguan Railway Bureau, went to Beijing a few days ago to discuss everything with the Ministries of Finance and Railways. After reaching an agreement with Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways, Li returned south yesterday. It is reported that three plans for the construction of the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section have been formulated as follows: (1) The original plan for the completion of the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section and the purchase of various locomotives for the Guangzhou-Shaoguan Railway will not be changed. (2) The original proposal to construct the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section from both ends simultaneously will be cancelled and changed to constructing directly from the south. It is now found that the section from Shaoguan to Liputou has been built and opened to traffic. The section from Liputou to Lechang is expected to be completed and opened to traffic in April of this year. At the end of April, construction will continue on the road from Lechang to Luojiadu (Luojiadu [blank space] is located in Pingshi). The engineering of this section of the road [blank space] can be opened for bidding during the day, and merchants have also arrived in Guangdong to prepare for bidding. (3) Regarding the issue of construction funds for the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan Railway this year, it is found that the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan Railway can be built to Luojiadu from March of this year to March of next year. The construction funds required during this year are about 7 million yuan. It has been decided that the Ministries of Railways and Finance will each allocate half of this amount. The remaining shortfall of about 1 million yuan will be the responsibility of the Guangdong Provincial Government and the Guangzhou-Shaoguan Railway Bureau to raise. (20th)

Northern Anhui

The Special Goods Office is Abolished

It Operated for Several Months Without Success

It Was Ordered to Close Immediately

Bengbu Correspondence: Feng Yafo, the Special Commissioner for the Collection and Transportation of Special Goods in Northern Anhui, came to Bengbu last winter and set up an office in Runfuli. He appointed a large number of collectors and transporters, who went to various counties to collect and transport goods in person. Their method of collection and transportation was entirely a policy of prohibition in the guise of taxation. It was called collection and transportation, but in reality, it was taxation. However, since the opening of the collection, due to the poor management of the office, more than three months have passed, and there have been no results. The quotas in each county are too heavy, with some reaching as high as 70,000 or 80,000 or more. At a time when the people are poor and resources are exhausted, there is no income, so very few county branches report monthly remittances. The head office only received several thousand yuan in guarantee deposits from the collectors and transporters in each county. The authorities were very dissatisfied with this and immediately ordered the abolition of the Special Goods Office in Northern Anhui. Feng Yafo was appointed as the Special Commissioner for the Investigation and Prohibition of Tobacco Seedlings in Anhui. Feng set up an office in Anqing to investigate and prohibit tobacco seedlings and specialized in investigating and prohibiting tobacco seedlings. He came to Bengbu from the province a few days ago to handle the closure of the Special Goods Office. After the closure was completed, he returned to the province with the important personnel of the head office. After the Special Goods Head Office was closed clearly, the Bengbu Inspection Office of this tobacco special goods depot and the branch offices in various counties in Northern Anhui were also ordered to close in order. It is reported that many collectors and transporters in each county suffered losses as a result. (23rd)

A Military and Police Inspectorate is Re-established in Bengbu

Responsible for Maintaining Public Security

Directly Under the Jurisdiction of the Garrison Department

Bengbu Correspondence: Since the Bengbu Garrison Headquarters was abolished and Xu Tingyao went north to participate in the war of resistance against Japan, the defense of this area has been undertaken by the 37th Regiment of the 19th Brigade of the 7th Division, commanded by Wang Kaizhen. However, the garrison matters of the Jinpu Railway are still the responsibility of Wang Jun, Commander of the Third Army. Wang believes that Bengbu is located in a strategic location on the Jinpu Railway, and the public security of the area is extremely important. There was previously a Military and Police Inspectorate in Bengbu, which was directly under the jurisdiction of the Jinpu Railway Garrison Headquarters. Now that the situation is unstable, the Military and Police Inspectorate should be restored as soon as possible. Therefore, Wang Kaizhen, Commander of the 37th Regiment stationed in Bengbu, was specially appointed as the concurrent Director of the Inspectorate. It will be organized immediately and is scheduled to take office before the 25th. Regarding the expenses, local consultations will be held, and at least 1,500 yuan will be required. Therefore, a special letter was sent to the Chamber of Commerce to discuss raising funds to facilitate the process. After receiving the letter, the Chamber of Commerce invited representatives from various agencies and public associations to a meeting at 3:00 pm on the 23rd to discuss the matter. As a result, it was agreed to undertake 1,000 yuan per month. The method of apportionment is that, in addition to an additional two yuan per geisha from the geisha singing donation, the rest will be undertaken by the tax collection agencies and major merchants separately. The amount apportioned by each bank will be undertaken by the Banking Association for 100 yuan, and the Chamber of Commerce will immediately inform Commander Wang of this by letter. (24th)

All Shanghai Organizations

Will Suggest a Wartime Organization to the Central Government

To Control the National Economy, Military Affairs, and Transportation

The Federation of All Chinese Industries is Currently Negotiating

The Federation of All Chinese Industries held a reception for public organizations and the press at the Bank Association Club at 5:00 pm yesterday to discuss and suggest that the Central Government establish a political center to control military, economic, and transportation affairs to facilitate the overall resistance against the enemy. The details of the various news items are recorded below.

Participating Public Organizations

Those who attended last night included representatives from the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Citizens' Federation, the Journalists' Association, the Federation of Machine-Made National Goods Factories, the Shipping Association, the Shanghai National Goods Factories Federation, and other organizations, as well as representatives from the Qingdao, Suzhou, and other branches of the Federation, totaling more than 20 people. They were warmly received by Qian Chengxu of the Federation and Lin Kanghou of the Federation of Chambers of Commerce.

Chairman's Speech

During the meeting, the Chairman said in his speech, "Fellow comrades, the guests today are either celebrities in the industrial and commercial circles or leaders from various regions. Discussing and consulting on the grand plan of resisting Japan and saving the nation can be said to be a rare opportunity. Today, we are facing a major national crisis. First, we must ask ourselves, from the standpoint of the people, whether it is industry or commerce, or other professions, whether we want to save the country. Second, if we want to save the country, in the current emergency and serious situation, how can we save the country? I have carefully considered these two points, and the current situation in China presents this phenomenon: on the part of the masses, there is a lack of unity, so the various organizations cannot be very strong. In the political aspect, the distribution of powers is too fragmented, so the power of the center cannot be generated to deal with this special crisis. However, adversity builds a nation. There is this lesson from ancient times. A nation must be able to devise a solution based on its own position and circumstances in order to save itself. The situation in China is exactly like this. From a positive point of view, it can be said that it is not a phenomenon of national subjugation, but a sign of national revival. The colleagues of our association have asked ourselves that, at such a serious time in the overall situation in China, we must do some work to save the country. Therefore, a few days ago, after everyone gathered to discuss, we formulated a draft telegram to be submitted to the Central Government, advocating that the Central Government transform the current government into a wartime organization, concentrate powers, and control military, economic, and transportation affairs to facilitate the overall external response. However, from our own standpoint, the Federation of All Chinese Industries is purely an industrial group. This type of work and design for saving the country is of great importance and cannot be undertaken by relying on the strength of a local organization. Therefore, I have specially invited various public organizations tonight and for the next two days, and at the same time, I will present this draft to ask the guests present to seriously discuss and vote on it, and also ask the guests present to publicly elect a chairman to preside over tonight's meeting, etc."

Results of Discussion

After the various organizations discussed on the spot, they passed the principle and advocated that after the Federation of All Chinese Industries first receives various public organizations next Monday, they will then schedule another tea party to discuss the final steps to make a strong recommendation to the government.

Key Points of the Proposal

The association decided to hold a general meeting after receiving various public organizations on the 28th and 29th to pass a proposal to the Central Government to change the government into a wartime organization. The proposal (1) advocates that a person be appointed to be responsible for controlling the military, training elite troops, and implementing a national military deployment plan to defend against the enemy. (2) The Central Government should make overall plans to organize a wartime financial institution outside the wartime government to control the national economy. (3) Organize a military transportation agency to control national transportation.

Zhu Qinglan Talks About Determination to Resist the Enemy

Recovering Lost Territory Is Not Difficult

The Volunteer Army in the East is Active and Waiting for an Opportunity to Move

This Time He is Here to Negotiate Relief for Northeastern Refugees

General Zhu [illegible character] Xian, recently seeing the expansion of the anti-Japanese military in North China, and the increasing number of refugees in the Northeast, and the need for huge amounts of funds for resettlement, which cannot be collected from one corner of the north, specially came south to negotiate with various charitable organizations in Shanghai, in order to achieve great results. Zhu arrived in Shanghai last night. The reporter specially visited Zhu at his private residence this morning. The following is a record of Zhu's remarks:

Negotiating for Relief for Refugees Zhu first said that he came here entirely to provide relief for refugees in the north, because after the fall of Rehe and the three eastern provinces, refugees from various places are increasingly concentrated in Pingjin and other places, and the war is expanding day by day, and wounded soldiers are also being transported to the rear one after another. The resettlement matters require huge expenses, so I personally came to Shanghai to negotiate with various circles in Shanghai, and plan to invite some people to help in the north. I will return north as soon as the negotiations are settled.

The Volunteer Army is Active and Waiting to Move The people in the Northeast are suffering unspeakable pain under the iron heel of the enemy. They look forward to the government being able to recover the non-land. Although the Japanese army is frequently invading, as long as the hearts of the people across the country do not die, and they are determined to resist, there is no fear that they will not be able to recover the lost territory. Therefore, the volunteer army in the hinterland of the eastern provinces is active, and if they get an opportunity, they can rise up at any time.

The Battle Situation on the Front is Very Good As for the battle situation on the front, the situation has been very good recently, because the troops are mostly determined to die, and everywhere they can use a very small number of troops to intercept the enemy unexpectedly. There was once a Big Sword Team soldier who cut down ten enemies in a row, resulting in his injury. As for the supply to the front, due to the inconvenience of transportation, there are indeed many difficulties in reality, but the rear must decide on a fundamental solution to provide supply. Recently, when Song Zheyuan's troops were fighting, at a time of emergency in the war, the transportation of food to the front was entirely done by local residents, etc.

Can Arrive in Shanghai Today

Various Organizations Jointly Go to the Wharf to Welcome

The Nissin Company's Ships

Internal Decision on Shipping Routes

[A total of seven lines, none of which are commercially viable]

According to the Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun, the seven shipping routes of the Nissin Company, centered on Shanghai, have been hit by extreme anti-Japanese sentiment and the conflict between the Chinese and Japanese armies. The business has been increasingly declining since this year. Since April of last year, the number of voyages on the designated shipping routes in one year was about 230, but in reality, it was less than 100. However, the designated shipping routes, which are usually changed in April every year, have been internally decided by the Ministry of Communications as follows: (1) Shanghai-Hankou Line, four ships, more than 120 voyages. (2) Hankou-Yichang Line, two ships, 48 voyages. (3) Hankou-Xiangtan Line, one ship, 24 voyages. (4) Shanghai-Tianjin Line, two ships, 36 voyages. (5) Shanghai-Guangdong Line, two ships, 36 voyages. (6) Yichang-Chongqing Line, one ship, number of voyages not determined. (7) Hankou-Changde Line, one ship, number of voyages not determined. The Hankou-Yichang, Hankou-Xiangtan, Tianjin-Shanghai, Shanghai-Guangdong, Yichang-Chongqing, and Hankou-Changde lines all have no business to speak of.

Yu Youren Arrived in Shanghai This Morning

His Foot Ailment Has Relapsed, and He Has Come to Shanghai for Medical Treatment

He Will Return to Beijing as Soon as He Recovers Slightly

Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, left Beijing by night train last night and arrived at the North Station at about 8:00 am this morning. He immediately returned to his residence to rest. According to Yu's attendants, Yu has long suffered from dampness in his feet. It relapsed this time in Beijing, making it difficult to move, so he came to Shanghai for medical treatment. He will return to Beijing as soon as he recovers slightly.

Gu Mengyu Returned to Beijing This Morning

Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, and Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways, representing the Central Government, came to Shanghai one after another to persuade Wang Jingwei to return to his position as President of the Executive Yuan. Sun accompanied Wang to Beijing last night. Gu, due to other important matters, delayed until 9:00 am this morning before taking the No. 04 flower car attached to the express train to return to Beijing.

Order from the Trademark Bureau

Improving Cotton Classification Standards

He Zhuoxian, Director of the Trademark Bureau, believes that there are different grades and varieties of white cotton in China. There are five main standards. When the China Cotton Production Improvement Association held a meeting in Beijing a few days ago, Director Ye was sent to Beijing to participate, and brought rough [illegible character] standard one [illegible character] and various [illegible character] to attend, soliciting opinions from experts on the grades tried and set by the bureau. After detailed discussion by the experts, it was felt that the names of the various standards were still not very perfect. Therefore, after Director Ye returned to the bureau this time, he specially ordered the standard names to be improved as follows: (1) Lingbao Long-Staple American Cotton Grade Standard was changed to Long-Staple American Cotton Grade Standard. (2) American Cotton Grade Standard was changed to Short-Staple American Cotton Grade Standard. (3) Black-Seeded Fine Lint Grade Standard was changed to Black-Seeded Medium Cotton Grade Standard. (4) White-Seeded Coarse Lint Grade Standard was changed to White-Seeded Medium Cotton Grade Standard. (5) Tianjin Hard Lint Grade Standard was changed to Special Hard Lint Grade Standard.

Bad Weather

Difficult to Rescue the Yutong Ship

The First and Second Holds are 15 Feet Underwater

The Ship's Passenger and Cargo Losses Total 260,000

The Yutong Ship of the Yu Da Shipping Company ran aground near Xinghua, Fujian. The ship is sinking, and the situation is extremely critical. It seems that it will be impossible to rescue. The total loss of passengers and cargo on the ship is about 260,000 yuan. The details are recorded below.

Critical Situation The Yu Da Shipping Company received a telegram from the Xinghua Branch this morning stating that the bottom of the front hold of the Yutong Ship has broken, and seawater has entered the first and second holds, increasing from 13 feet to 15 feet. The ship's draft is five feet when the tide is low. The engine room and the rear hold are unharmed. Due to bad weather, rescue [illegible character]. Currently, Lianbao Shui [illegible character] Company has commissioned a Japanese salvage company to send a ship from Moji to the accident site to rescue. It is scheduled to [illegible character] tonight.

Total Loss of Passengers and Cargo The Coast Guard of the Military Department sent a patrol ship from Xiamen to the accident site, which arrived last night. It is stationed next to the Yutong Ship at the accident site to prevent pirates from robbing it. As for the crew of the ship, although they have been rescued, the 1,700 tons of passengers and cargo, soybean cakes, etc., worth 120,000 yuan, are completely wet and swollen, and it is impossible to load and unload them. The price of the ship is about 140,000 yuan. Because the passengers and cargo cannot be loaded and unloaded, it is difficult to escape the danger in reality, and it has already sunk. The insurance companies of Dalian for the passengers and cargo have sent personnel to inspect.

The Monastery's Meditation Hall Turns Into an Opium Den

Three Sets of Opium Smoking Equipment Seized Inside Bao Lao Ye Temple

More Than Ten Young Women Also Found Inside the Temple

| Abbot Zhang Wenyu and Others Sentenced to One Month Imprisonment Each |

Inside Bao Lao Ye Temple, located at No. 542-3 Tunan Lane, North Henan Road, reside more than thirty monks. The abbot, Zhang Wenyu, is deeply addicted to opium. Recently, this abbot, seeing that most of the monks in the temple shared his addiction, prepared extra opium equipment to prevent profits from flowing elsewhere. He set up a secret den in a more secluded monk's room, so they could all enjoy the taste of "sweet dew." Thus, besides chanting sutras every day, they only indulged in smoking opium. This was discovered by Inspector Yao Jialin of District C, who believed that turning a monastery meditation hall into an opium den was a severe violation of the law. He petitioned the First Special District Local Court for a search warrant and, on the afternoon of the other day, braved the rain to search the temple. Most of the monks were out, and only the abbot, along with incense caretakers Xiao Dexing, Pan Bosheng, and Guo Chunlai, were lying on the bed, indulging in their addiction. They were all arrested, and three sets of opium equipment, two jars of opium paste, and sixty-nine rolls of dried opium were seized. At that time, more than ten young women suddenly appeared inside the temple. Inspector Yao Jialin, seeing that they did not resemble ordinary worshippers, questioned them suspiciously. The women confessed in unison that they were all wives of the monks in the temple. For monks who were supposed to have emptied the five skandhas and purified the six senses, to suddenly have beautiful wives living with them in the monastery was truly unheard of. This further demonstrated the temple's usual practice of harboring filth and hiding dirt. After witnessing this strange phenomenon, Inspector Yao Jialin sneered at it and immediately took Zhang Wenyu and the other three, along with the opium equipment, back to the police station. Yesterday, they were brought before Judge Huang Risheng of the First Special District Local Court for interrogation. Lawyers Li Zhishan and Zhang Shizhu from the police station stated that the defendants would be prosecuted for violating Article 11 of the Anti-Opium Law. Subsequently, Inspector Yao Jialin reported the details of the case, and when asked by Judge Huang, the defendants Zhang Wenyu and others confessed to smoking opium without denial. Judge Huang then sentenced the four defendants, Zhang, Xiao, Pan, and Guo, to one month imprisonment each, and confiscated the opium paste and opium equipment.

Public Security Bureau Regulations

Procedures for Handling Unidentified Corpses

| Circular Order to All District Stations to Comply |

Wen Hongen, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, recently issued a circular order to all district police captains, stating that in order to ensure compliance, it has been found that the reporting procedures for unidentified corpses discovered within the jurisdiction of each district station are inconsistent, and the sizes of corpse photographs also vary, as do the reported photography costs. Unless proper measures are established and uniformly enforced, it will be insufficient to ensure uniformity and demonstrate prudence. Eight procedures for handling unidentified corpses discovered within the jurisdiction of each district station have now been established. In addition to separate orders and distribution, a copy of these procedures is hereby issued to all district stations for immediate compliance. This order.

Handling Procedures (1) When each district station discovers an unidentified corpse within its jurisdiction, it shall immediately report to the local court in accordance with the law for personnel to inspect it, take photographs, and immediately report to this Bureau. (2) Fingerprints shall be taken from the victim's corpse, and eight photographs shall be taken, one to be kept by the district station for public announcement and claim, and the remaining seven, one each to be kept by the Records Section and the Fingerprint Section, one to be posted at the Bureau's entrance for public recognition, and four to be sent to major newspapers for public recognition, along with the fingerprint paper, to be sent to the Bureau with a prepared document and a homicide investigation form to be sent to the Third Section for reference. (3) For corpses that died of illness, seven photographs shall be taken, one to be kept by the district station for public announcement and claim, and the remaining six, one each to be kept by the Records Section and one to be posted at the Bureau's entrance for public recognition, and four to be sent to major newspapers for public recognition, to be sent to the Bureau with a prepared document. Fingerprints need not be taken for corpses that died of illness, and a homicide investigation form need not be filled out. (4) If the victim died in a water, fire, or vehicle accident, a homicide investigation form shall be filled out and reported to the Third Section, and seven photographs shall be taken, with six sent with a prepared document, but fingerprints need not be taken. (5) The corpse must be photographed from the front, with the face clearly visible. Except for the body, no other scenery needs to be included. (6) The size of the photographs shall be four inches. (7) The price of eight photographs shall not exceed three yuan at most. (8) If the location of the corpse is far from the photography studio, car fare may be appropriately reimbursed.

Special Issue on the Lives of Female Employees (II)

Casual Chats by Ye Yu

Words from a "Weaver"

— Zhi

Five minutes before going to press, I calculated the number of words in the manuscripts compiled for this issue, and it was still four hundred and fifty words short. Naturally, this requires us editors to "weave" some more.

Several readers have written to us seeking our opinions on improving the lives of female workers and female employees. This puts us in a bit of a difficult position:

First, in this era where mentioning workers and employees immediately conjures up thoughts of "left-leaning" and "right-leaning," it is very difficult to speak. You must at least weigh your words on a scale before you can say them, otherwise, you will either be accused of "tailism" or "left-wing infantile disorder," or someone will say that you are a "backward person of the times!"

Second, the universal spread of the world economic panic has made the lives of the general working masses increasingly impoverished. All the Hoover saints and all the MacDonalds, despite exhausting various methods of improvement and relief, still cannot solve the unemployment problem and other livelihood issues in the slightest. Then, needless to say, the humble editors like us are even less capable. I know I can avoid playing an axe in front of Lu Ban!

In short, if female employees want to alleviate their own suffering, they can only turn to themselves and rely on their own continuous efforts and struggles. Others cannot do it for them. Moreover, the social science that female employees learn from their own life struggles is much richer and more accurate than what we editors sitting in the library learn every day! Dear readers! Do you want to know the secret to improving your lives? I'll tell you, please go ask the great gentlemen!

Life of the Masses

Prison

— Ms. Yi Ling

Female Telephone Operator

I used to work as a telephone operator in a concession telephone company in a certain port. Many women envied this profession, thinking that we led a happy life. But this is because they don't know the inside story, and they don't know how much pain and humiliation we suffered there!

Although our working hours are not as long as those of female factory workers, we have to do more than seven hours of monitored work every day. As soon as we run into the company, we feel like we have entered a prison. We work like machines all day long, without a minute to be lazy. Being five minutes late results in half a day's pay being deducted. In the switchboard room where I worked, there were seven or eight foreign female "Four Nine Nine" and a dozen Chinese female "Four Nine Nine." "Four Nine Nine" means supervisor. They are like foremen in a factory, patrolling around all day long. If they see anyone being lazy or talking, they will scold you or tell the manager. The manager will immediately call you in and give you a big lecture.

Our manager is a tall and thin American woman. She is very strict. Her seat is in the center, looking around and monitoring us. She has a receiver on her desk. Her receiver is different from the switchboard operator's receiver, but the same as the ordinary telephone user's receiver. But her receiver has special uses. When she puts the receiver to her ear, she can immediately know which station is talking among the hundreds of us. Once, a colleague talked to a man outside for a few words. It happened that the manager was listening to the receiver at this time. She heard it, and immediately stood up and sneaked behind the colleague like a mouse, and pulled her shoulders hard with both hands, which startled the colleague. The colleague turned around and saw that it was the manager, and her face turned red. The manager asked her what she was doing, and then called her over and scolded her in front of everyone. Finally, she spoke in broken Shanghai dialect: "Be careful, be careful!"

This is an imperialist money-making machine, the best example of imperialist exploitation. Although we only have ten or twenty yuan a month, we have to deduct wages for taking leave here: half a day's leave deducts a full day's pay; one day's leave deducts three days' pay; sick leave deducts half a day's pay, and it must be certified by a designated hospital.

Another thing that is most heartbreaking is that even urinating is restricted. You have to report to "Four Nine Nine" when you urinate. The time is only allowed for five minutes, and defecation is also only allowed for five minutes! Running from the work station to the staircase, and from the staircase to the toilet on the second floor takes two or three minutes. The limit of five minutes is really not enough. If someone goes to the toilet a few more times due to physical discomfort, the manager will call her in for questioning again. But the manager and foreign staff on the second floor don't have to run up the stairs, and their time is not restricted. But no matter who they are, they always spend more than ten minutes in the toilet each time. This is probably because their physiological structure is somewhat different from ours!

I worked so hard for three years, until the company installed automatic machines, and the January 28th Incident happened at this time. The company took the opportunity of our escape to dismiss us, so as to avoid us asking for unemployment compensation. In this way, my switchboard operator's life came to an end.

Amateur Cafe

Female Store Clerks and Abortion

— Wu Wenbo

Because I studied medicine, I hung up a sign as a gynecologist in the French Concession. Once, I performed an abortion for a female employee of Company ×, who had severe lung disease and was not suitable for childbearing. From then on, many female store clerks came to discuss this issue. But I had been a criminal defendant for performing abortions before. The judge scolded me, saying: You say that female workers cannot work without abortions, and cannot eat without work. Moreover, the pregnancy is not yet three months old, and there is no danger to the adult if it is aborted, so I gave it to her. But that is Soviet law, not Chinese law. Therefore, I sat in jail for three months. Since then, when female store clerks come to me to discuss this matter, I refuse and say: Give birth to it this time, and a little baby is also very cute. If you don't want to give birth next time, I can think of a way. You should come and discuss it with me earlier. But they are all determined to "think of a way this time, and don't worry about it next time," and because my clinic is relatively clean, and the fees are very low, there are still people who come to discuss it.

From my old doctor's point of view, although female store clerks are said to be economically independent working women, once they have a lover, if I am not around to interfere, before long the crystallization of love will start to act strangely in their stomachs, and they will feel that they are not as free as young ladies from wealthy families, and they will be busy looking for a solution. This is because economically independent working women are not really independent. The salary that the company gives them is to make them wear a few more beautiful clothes to set off their beauty in order to attract customers, not their real salary. The company will never provide them with all the pre- and post-natal expenses, so their lives are not much different from those of female workers. It is no wonder that they all ask me like this: "So, what should I do with the thing in my stomach?" But I can only answer them like this: "Miss, to borrow the words of the Chinese judge who imprisoned me for three months, please go to the Soviet Union!"

said that the right hand wanted to shake my left hand.

"Sir, behave yourself, what else do you want to eat?" I gave him a "nail."

"I can't believe you, you have such a big attitude. Okay, just bring me anything, whiskey, sandwich, butter toast... bring me whatever you want, anyway, I have plenty of money in my pocket." He was a little embarrassed and angry, wanting to use money to overwhelm people, but I still gave him a cold shoulder.

But the boss knew about this. He said that I offended the customer, which would affect his business, so he earnestly taught me a lesson. He said:

"Customers pay money to eat, not to be insulted. They have money, and we also want money. If he asks you how old you are, you tell him how old you are. If he wants to hold you and touch you, you let him hold you and touch you, there is nothing big deal about it. Otherwise, where would you get your big tips, which are several times your monthly salary? If my employees all offended customers like you, wouldn't my store be visited by ghosts? Think about it, wouldn't our store have to close? If it closes, where would you get your big tips, which are several times your monthly salary? So I advise you, don't be so stupid in the future. Whatever they want you to do, you do it. Holding and touching won't cause you any loss anyway..."

"Yes, I am stupid. I can't do such a shameless thing. I can't let them tease me at will. I can't fawn on them." I interrupted the boss before he could continue and answered him simply like that.

"If you work as a waitress in my place, you have to do this. If you don't do it, then please find another job and do what you want to do!" He threatened me with closing the business.

I didn't say anything, and tears streamed down like rain.

Self-Professional Introduction

A Retinue of Bodyguards

— Ms. Hai Xiao

Female Civil Servant

Not sitting in the boudoir to embroider phoenixes, I travel to foreign lands for a living, weathering frost and snow, my rosy face withers, my aspirations are not realized, only a sliver remains.

Editor: Thank you. Could you please publish this letter of mine?

I am a civil servant in a certain political organization, but I don't have a retinue of bodyguards because I am not an important person, and I am now considered "retired." Now I enclose a poem and a painting. Please put the poem in front of this letter and the painting in the back. These shallow works, surrounded by a retinue, will be my bodyguards, but I need you to take the time to "inspect" them!

I am from Zhejiang, in my twenties, a graduate of the university's art department. I am skilled in poetry, painting, sculpture, crafts, and Chinese shorthand. I have served as a civil servant, lawyer's assistant, speech stenographer, middle school dean, director of student affairs, Chinese and art teacher, female student instructor, and private tutor. Currently, I am an art teacher in a certain middle school, but I only teach eight hours a week. I am willing to contribute to society in my spare time. Please forward any "response" through your publication.

The United Front of the Boss and the Honored Guest

— Ms. Yun Ling

Waitress in a Coffee Shop

Having worked as a waitress in ××× for more than twenty days, I have tasted all the unfairness of life. What is written below is one of the things I experienced in these twenty-odd days.

The sound of leather shoes "kak-kak" echoed on the stairs. A young man came in, wearing a gorgeous suit, with snow cream on his face and Stanco on his head. This is what my consciousness told me: I had to go forward to greet him.

"Sir, please sit here, what would you like to eat?" In order to solve the problem of food and clothing, I had to endure humiliation and engage in this disguised selling of smiles! A waitress, to serve these young masters and ruffians.

"A cup of coffee!"

While drinking, this young man kept looking at me and laughing to himself. "What is your name?" he asked me.

"My surname is ×." I replied to him simply.

"You look very pretty. How old are you this year?" This ignorant guy asked me further. Seeing that his eyes were flickering with malicious intent, I ignored him.

"Did you hear me? I asked you how old you are this year?" Poor guy, he didn't even know that there was no coffee left in his cup, and he still wanted to put the cup in his mouth.

"Sir, would you like anything else to eat?" I asked him without looking at him directly.

"...I want to eat the red on your lips..." His sly little account came from where? If everyone I employed in my store offended customers like you, wouldn't my store be visited by even ghosts? Think about it, wouldn't our store have to close? If it closes, where would you get your big tips, which are several times your monthly salary? So I advise you, don't be so stupid in the future. Whatever they want you to do, you do it. Touching and holding won't cause you any loss anyway..."

"Yes, I am stupid. I can't do such a shameless thing. I can't let them tease me at will. I can't fawn on them." I didn't wait for the boss to continue and answered him frankly like that.

"If you work as a waitress in my place, you have to do this. If you don't do it, then please find another job and do what you want to do!" He threatened me with closing the business.

I didn't say anything, and tears streamed down like rain.

Their "Progressive Action" and My "Reactionary Action"

— Ms. Ai Lian

Female Employee of a Certain Political Organization

It has become a habit for me to read the newspaper every morning. One day, I suddenly discovered a section: "A certain large agency is recruiting two female employees, salary 25 to 35 yuan; middle school education or above, anyone can apply..." Of course, I am a university-educated person, and my qualifications are up to standard, and there is no need for any photos, so I boldly sent a resume. In less than three days, they sent me a mimeographed notice, asking me to go to a certain place to take the exam. I was too happy when I went. Indeed, I am very clear that this is a very famous, dignified government agency. One of my cousins once planned to go, but the person he asked for help was too small, so he failed. Unexpectedly, I easily stepped into this big iron gate. What I am afraid of is not being admitted. When I entered the examination hall, I further proved that I would definitely fail; because among the seventy or so candidates, I knew two who were graduates of a certain university, and one was a professor at my alma mater. In terms of my knowledge, there is little hope, and I have not asked anyone for help!

More than twenty proctors came, all standing. One of them gave a few words first. He said: There are too many of us, so we will switch to oral examinations. So one by one they were called in front of them to ask questions. What they asked, I couldn't hear, but I saw that the twenty or so people were constantly recording in their hands. I didn't understand what they were recording. Does one person's answer require so many people to take notes? Later, they called my name. In addition to some of the information already on the resume, they only asked one more question: "Are you married?"

Quickly, the next afternoon, a letter came. Contrary to anyone's expectations, I was admitted.

I went, and I found that another person who was admitted was a very beautiful person who was about my age. Her surname is Liu. The salary was explained; she was 25 yuan, and I was 35 yuan. From this time on, the secret of the exam had not yet been broken, but another period of mysterious life began!

A week passed, but I didn't handle a single official matter. I always brought a few novels to read every day, spending seven or eight hours. I hadn't signed the attendance book either, because they said that female employees didn't need to sign in. So it didn't matter if I was late, left early, or didn't come at all. As long as a male colleague had nothing to do, he would come to my desk to chat, which was really annoying! They knew that I liked to read novels, so I often found books they gave me in my drawer. I didn't know who bought them, or who to return them to? This made me extremely embarrassed! After a few more days, we got to know each other a little better, and they asked me to dinner, dancing, movies, etc., but I always refused. In order to avoid them bothering me, I always asked my older brother, who worked at the customs, to pick me up when I went home. So some male colleagues hated me a little. There was no opportunity in the office; when I left the office, my brother was waiting for me, they were really helpless.

Ms. Liu, she sat far away from me. I thought she was more knowledgeable than me, she knew how to deal with the world. Playful voices were constantly transmitted to my ears. After leaving the office, there were always two or three male colleagues walking with her. It is said that watching movies is a daily routine. Dancing and suppers are also very common. Once, she even played mahjong all night with five colleagues at × Hotel. For her, it may be that she had to deal with the job for the sake of making a living, and she was at ease with it. At the same time, she could also take advantage of a good opportunity to seek her own pleasure. However, I always disliked her a little, so I rarely talked to her. She asked me to dinner several times, although she declared that there would be no third person with us, but I always declined!

On Sunday morning of the third week after entering a certain agency, Ms. Liu suddenly came to visit me at my residence. Although I had never received colleagues who came to find me, Ms. Liu was a female colleague, and it was her first time, so I was embarrassed to refuse her, so I finally invited her in. She sent me a
